/*
 * only used for RapidSpell spell checker when directly checking an rte area
 * use the attribute: textComponentInterface="Custom"
 * when using the RapidSpell custom tag
 */
function RSCustomInterface(tbElementName){
  this.tbName = tbElementName;
  this.getText = getText;
  this.setText = setText;
  function getText(){
     
        return window[this.tbName].getValue();
     
  }
  function setText(text){
    //set the text in the text component to the text argument
    //this may be HTML formatted text
    
          window[this.tbName].setValue(text);
    
  }
}

function ifOverflowElse(ifHTML, elseHTML) { 
    if (isOverflowSupported()) {
      document.write(ifHTML);
    } else {
      document.write(elseHTML);
    } 
}

<script type="text/javascript">


function scrollIt() {

    var spanny = document.getElementById("scrollarea");
    if(spanny) {
      spanny.scrollTop = 0;
    } else {
      window.scrollTo(0,0);
    }

}

/**
Save the current scroll position for form refreshing
*/
function recordScrollPosition(form) {
  form = getWorkFormForScrollPosition(form);
  var pos = getScrollPosition(form);
  if(form && form.bplte_p_scrollpos) {
     form.bplte_p_scrollpos.value = pos;
  }
  return true;
}

/**
Get current Form. If no form input, then first form default.
*/
function getWorkFormForScrollPosition(form) {
  if(form == null){
  form = document.getElementsByTagName('form')[0];
  }
  if(typeof(form) == 'string'){
  form = document.getElementById(form);
  }
  return form;
}

/** 
Get the current form scroll position.
*/
function getScrollPosition(form)
{
  form = getWorkFormForScrollPosition(form);
  var spanny, pos;
  if(form && form.bplte_p_scrollpos) {
    spanny = document.getElementById("scrollarea");
    if(spanny) {
      pos = spanny.scrollTop;
    } else {
      
      // The below code of document.documentElementis to support for ( firefox & IE - other such browsers) | document.body.scrollTop is for chrome browser
      if (document.documentElement && (document.documentElement.scrollTop > document.body.scrollTop)) {
      	pos = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
      } else {
      	pos = document.body.scrollTop;
      }
      
      if (pos === undefined) {
        pos = window.pageYOffset;
      }
    }
  }
  return pos;
}

</script>



<script type="text/javascript">


  scrollFunction = scrollIt;


function bodyOnLoad()
{
  loadTimes.push({name:"pre-onload", ms:(new Date()|0)-tpreload});
  ttotal0 = new Date()|0;

  tmaf0 = new Date()|0;
  measureAllFields();
  tmaf1 = new Date()|0;
  loadTimes.push({
    name:"measureAllFields()",
    ms:tmaf1-tmaf0
  });
  
}

</script>

<input type="hidden" name="xsc_fields" value=" ">

<script type="text/javascript">

// set form object for spell check
function setSpellCheckForm(form) {
	spellCheckForm = form;
}

// performs spell check for whole form
function openSpellCheckForm(finishFunc)
{
	spellCheckForm.xsc_fields.value = " ";
	
	if (finishFunc != undefined ) 
	   xsc.popup(spellCheckForm, finishFunc);
	else
	   xsc.popup(spellCheckForm, "void(0)");
	   
}

// performs spell check for specified fields
function openSpellCheckFormFields(fieldNamesToCheck)
{		
	spellCheckForm.xsc_fields.value = fieldNamesToCheck;
	xsc.popup(spellCheckForm);
}

// performs spell check for 1 text area
function openSpellCheckInput(inputName)
{
	var contents = document.getElementById(inputName).value;

	if (isWhitespace(contents)) {
		alert('No content inserted for spell check.');
	} else {
		spellCheckForm.xsc_fields.value = inputName;
		xsc.popup(spellCheckForm);
	}
}

// performs spell check for whole form
function openSpellCheckFormWithForm(form)
{
	form.xsc_fields.value = " ";
	xsc.popup(form);
}

// performs spell check for 1 text area
function openSpellCheckInputWithForm(form, inputName)
{
	var contents = document.getElementById(inputName).value;

	if (isWhitespace(contents)) {
		alert('No content inserted for spell check.');
	} else {
		form.xsc_fields.value = inputName;
		xsc.popup(form);
	}
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

setSpellCheckForm(document.forms[0]);

</script>

function showPrintWindow(title, url) {
  var form = document.forms[0];
  var modified = isFormModified(form);
  // RCM-4401 add security scrumb otherwise print preview won't work
  var newurl = "/rcmprintpreview?"+url+"&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey;
  
 
  var wnd = window.open(modified?"":newurl, "rcmprintpreview", "menubar,scrollbars,toolbar=1,resizable,height=480,outerHeight=560,width=730");
  wnd.focus();
  try {
    wnd.resizeTo(730, 560);
  } catch (e) {}

  if (modified) {
    wnd.document.write(
      "<HTML><TITLE>Print Preview</TITLE>"+
      "<link type='text/css' rel='stylesheet' href='/ui/uicore/css/V10Classes_9ab89be4f2ee5f77f470f59ab6813587.css' />"+
      "<"+"BODY"+"><P class='pm-form-title' style='text-align:center'>"+title+"</P>"+
      "<P class='bodytext' style='text-align:center'>Auto-Saving...</P></"+"BODY"+">"+
      "</HTML>");

    form.elements['bplte_rcmpreviewurl'].value = newurl;
    recordScrollPosition(form);
    form.submit();
    

  }
}

function showPrintPreview(ppDraftId, ppFolderMapId, ppFormDataId, ppTime, ppToken, formOwnerId, calSessionId) {
  var url = "";
  
  if (ppDraftId != null && ppDraftId != '')
    url = "bplte_company=ICRCTEST1&pp_pm_draftid="+ppDraftId+"&pp_pm_mode=pp_pm_mode_printall&pp_pm_tm="+ppTime+"&pp_pm_tk="+ppToken+"&pp_pm_owner="+formOwnerId+"&pp_cal_session_id="+calSessionId;
  else if (ppFolderMapId != null && ppFolderMapId != '') {
    url = "bplte_company=ICRCTEST1&pp_pm_fmapid="+ppFolderMapId+"&pp_pm_mode=pp_pm_mode_printall&pp_pm_tm="+ppTime+"&pp_pm_tk="+ppToken+"&pp_pm_owner="+formOwnerId+"&pp_cal_session_id="+calSessionId;
    
    
    

}
  else if (ppFormDataId != null && ppFormDataId != '')
    url = "bplte_company=ICRCTEST1&pp_pm_fdataid="+ppFormDataId+"&pp_pm_mode=pp_pm_mode_printall&pp_pm_tm="+ppTime+"&pp_pm_tk="+ppToken+"&pp_pm_owner="+formOwnerId+"&pp_cal_session_id="+calSessionId;

  showPrintWindow('Print Preview', url+"&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey);
}

function warn_on_deletedoc() {
  var warn_msg = "Are you sure you want to delete the document?";
  if (confirm(warn_msg))
    return true;
  else
    return false;
}

  var warn_msg = "Are you sure you want to delete this competency?";
  if (confirm(warn_msg))
    return true;
  else
    return false;
}

  s.click();
  return false;
}

<script type="text/javascript">

var rteIDs = new Array();

function checkRTEComment() {
    var keyButton = gebi('fb2toolbar_button_field');
    if (keyButton) {
        if (keyButton.value == 'fb2toolbar_btn_close_without_save') {
            return true; // skip check when close without save
        }
    }
    var isAutoSave = false;
    if (document.forms && document.forms[0] && document.forms[0].fb_auto_save_pm_logout) {
        var autoLogoutValue = document.forms[0].fb_auto_save_pm_logout.value;
        if (autoLogoutValue == 'T' || autoLogoutValue == 'F') {
            isAutoSave = true;
        }
    }
    var needConfirm = isAutoSave ? false : true;
    for (var indexI=0, len = rteIDs.length; indexI < len; indexI++) {
        var keyTemp = 'juic_RTEditor_alt_' + rteIDs[indexI];
        var rte = window[keyTemp];
        if (rte) {
            if (rte.isOverTextCountLimit()) {
                if (needConfirm) { 
                    if (!confirm("One or more text boxes on this page contain too much text. Click Cancel to return to the form and edit, OK to automatically remove the text and save the form.")) {
                        return false;
                    }
                    needConfirm = false;
                }
                rte.textLimiterAutoTrim();
                gebi(rteIDs[indexI] + "_hasChanged").value = "true";
            } else {
                //PMT-4824 RTE comment tidying to eliminate invalid/mismatch HTML tag      
                //Check if RTE comment is changed when click routing bar button
                if (rte.hasValueChanged()) {
                    gebi(rteIDs[indexI] + "_hasChanged").value = "true";
                } else {
                    gebi(rteIDs[indexI] + "_hasChanged").value = "false";
                }
            }
        }
    }
    return true;
}

}

<script type="text/javascript">

    window.localeForRapidSpellWeb = 'ENGLISH';
    document.onreadystatechange = function() {
      if (this.readyState === "complete") {
        var toolbarTabs = document.querySelectorAll(".contextualIcons .formButton_ui5");
        toolbarTabOperations(toolbarTabs);	
      }
    }; 
    function toolbarTabOperations(toolbarTabs) {
      var defaultFocus = document.querySelector(".contextualIcons .formButton_ui5.pressed");
      if (!defaultFocus) {
        defaultFocus = document.querySelector(".contextualIcons .formButton_ui5");
      }
      for(var i=0; i<toolbarTabs.length; i++){
        toolbarTabs[i].setAttribute("tabindex","-1");
        toolbarTabs[i].addEventListener("keydown",function(event){
			      var idx = getTabIndex(event.currentTarget.id, toolbarTabs);	
			        switch (event.key) {
			          case 'ArrowLeft':
			          case 'ArrowUp' :
						    if(idx > 0){
							    event.preventDefault();
					        juic.$(toolbarTabs[idx]).setAttribute("tabindex","-1")
					        juic.$(toolbarTabs[idx-1]).setAttribute("tabindex","0")
					        SFDom.setFocus(juic.$(toolbarTabs[idx-1].id));
					      }
			            break;
			
			          case 'ArrowRight':
			          case 'ArrowDown':
							  if(idx < toolbarTabs.length-1){
					          event.preventDefault();
						        juic.$(toolbarTabs[idx]).setAttribute("tabindex","-1")
						        juic.$(toolbarTabs[idx+1]).setAttribute("tabindex","0")
						        SFDom.setFocus(juic.$(toolbarTabs[idx+1].id));
						      }
			            break;
			          default:
			            break;
			        }
			    
        });
		    function getTabIndex(currentTabId, toolbarTabs){
		      var indx = null;
		      for(var i=0; i<toolbarTabs.length; i++){
		        if (currentTabId === toolbarTabs[i].id){
		          indx = i;
		        }
		      }
		      return indx;
		    };
      }
      defaultFocus.removeAttribute("tabindex");
    };

</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">

    var jobReqFormHandler = {};
    jobReqFormHandler.handleMenuItemClick = function(event) {
      var workflowButtonVO = event.button;
      if(workflowButtonVO.onClickString) {
        var onClickFn = eval("(function(){" + workflowButtonVO.onClickString + "})");
        onClickFn();
      } else {
        for(var key in workflowButtonVO.fieldKeyValueMap) {
          Util.setFieldAndSubmit(key, workflowButtonVO.fieldKeyValueMap[key]);
        }
      }
  	};
    SFDOMEvent.ready(function() {
	      if (window["formDataRouteBar"]) {
	        var routeMapContainer = new SFRouteMapContainer(window["formDataRouteBar"]);
	        routeMapContainer.addEventListener('menuItemClicked', jobReqFormHandler, 'handleMenuItemClick');
	        routeMapContainer.render('routeMap');
	      }
	    });
  

</script>

          var tabRoleIdList = [];

<script type="text/javascript">


/* 
 * This function finds all the (div class="commentsArea") which wraps fb_sect_ui_comments.jsp
 * and adds a target="_new", unless the tag starts with "javascript:" like spellchecker, legal scan
 * and waca. Also doesn't add the new target attribute if the tags parent className is "textAreaControls"
 * which happens when rich text editor is turned off and spellchecker, legal scan and waca are all
 * hyperlinks (anchor tags).
 */

var isCheckedCommentsArea = false; 
 
window.addEventListener("load",function() {
  if (isCheckedCommentsArea){
    return;
  }
  isCheckedCommentsArea = true;
  
  var cBoxes = SFDom.getElementsByClassName("commentsArea", "div");
  for (var i=0,len=cBoxes.length;i<len;++i) {
    var tags = cBoxes[i].getElementsByTagName("a");
	    for (var x=0,l=tags.length;x<l;++x) {
	    	if(tags[x].href.indexOf("javascript:") == -1){
	    		if(tags[x].parentNode.className != "textAreaControls"){
	      	 		tags[x].setAttribute("target","_new");
	      	 	}
	        }
	    }
  }
});

</script>

    }

<script type="text/javascript">


function _loadAttributes() {
	var key_field_id = competencyInputFieldId, jobReqId = jobRequisitionId, attributeType = jobReqAttributeType, locale = userSelectedLocale, config = competencyConfig;
	this.inputId = key_field_id;
	var controller = AjaxService.getMBeanInstance('jobReqController');
	        
	controller.getWSMCompetenciesForJobReq(jobReqId, attributeType, locale, {
	 	callback : function(response) {
			if (response) {
				if(response.validationErrors) {
					_setHiddenInputValue("ERROR");
					var competencyHolder = juic.$("wsmCompetencies");
					if(response.validationMessages.length) {
						var errorStr=[];
						response.validationMessages.forEach(function(errorMsg) {
							errorStr.push("<div class='redAlert'>", errorMsg, "</div>");
						});
						competencyHolder.innerHTML = errorStr.join('');
					}
				} else {
					var attributes = response.attributes || [];
					_setHiddenInputValue(JSON.stringify(attributes));
					_initializeRCMWSMAttributes(attributes, attributeType, locale, config);
				}
			}
	 	},
 	    exceptionHandler : function(msg, expObj) {
	 		_setHiddenInputValue("ERROR");
	 	},
     	errorHandler : function(err, msg) {
	 	    _setHiddenInputValue("ERROR");
	 	}
	});
}

function _setHiddenInputValue(value) {
	juic.$(this.inputId).value = value;
}

function _updateAttributesEventHandler (evt) {
	var selectedAttributes = evt.detail;

	_setHiddenInputValue(JSON.stringify(selectedAttributes));
}

function _initializeRCMWSMAttributes(attributesData, attributeType, locale, config) {
	//create a global variable to store updated competencies. The updated competencies used in AI JD widget
	window.competencies = attributesData.filter(function(attribute) {
		return attribute.libraryType === 'COMPETENCY';
  });
	var attributePickerConfig = {
			"attributeTypes": [
                {
                    "libraryTypeCode": attributeType
                }
            ],
			"userLocale": locale,
            "previouslySelectedAttributes": attributesData,
            "permissions": {
                "showFilter": true,
                "showTagFilter": true
            }
	};

	var fieldConfig = {
			readOnly: !config.editable,
			isInvalid: config.invalid
	};
	
	this.jobreqCompetency = new RCMWSMAttributes(attributePickerConfig, fieldConfig);

	var competencyHolder = juic.$("wsmCompetencies");

	if (competencyHolder) {
		this.jobreqCompetency.render('wsmCompetencies');
		this.jobreqCompetency.setAttributeItems(attributesData);

		// attach update event
		document.addEventListener("attributesModified", _updateAttributesEventHandler);
	}
}

// Stores the findUser objects which are later used to clear the values
var findUserObjectMap = new Map();

/*
 Clears the autocomplete search component values
 when the clear button is clicked on the edit
 Job Requisition Page
*/
function clearFindUserFields(fieldId) {
	var findUserObject = findUserObjectMap.get(fieldId);
	findUserObject._autoComp.setValue({userId: "", userDisplayValue: ""});
}
	
function renderFindUser(config){
	var divId = 'render' + config.divId + 'Search';
	var fieldIdArray = ["FIRST_NAME", "LAST_NAME", "USER_NAME", "DEPARTMENT", "LOCATION", "DIVISION", "USER_ROLE", "RBP_ROLES", "MATCH_TYPE"];
	if(config.groupId){
	   fieldIdArray.push("DYNAMIC_GROUPS." + String(config.groupId));
	}
	config.fieldIds = fieldIdArray;
	config.additionalCriteria = {};
	config.advancedSearchAdditionalCriteria = {};
	config.setUserId = true;
	var findUser = new RCMFindUser(config);
	findUserObjectMap.set(config.fieldId, findUser);
	findUser.render(divId);
}

/** contains field id as the key and array of rules as value which is assocaited  on onchange trigger **/
var ruleConfigMap = {"APCategory":["RM_COMPENDIUM"],"filter5":["Family"]};

/** map of field id and date picker component for date fiields. **/

/** Mapping object with dom id as key and template field id as value.this is reverse of "templateFieldIdDomFieldIdMap" object **/
var	domFieldIdTemplateFieldIdMap = {};


(function(){
	for (var key in templateFieldIdDomFieldIdMap){
		var value = templateFieldIdDomFieldIdMap[key];
		domFieldIdTemplateFieldIdMap[value] = key;
	}
})();

var triggerController = null;
var triggerBusinessRules  = function(element, obj) {
	if (ruleEnabled){ 
		if(triggerController) {
			triggerController.updateElemAndRuleObj(element, obj);
		} else {
		    triggerController = new RCMFireRuleOnChangeController(element, obj, "JobReq");
		}
		triggerController.triggerRule();
	}
}

var effectiveDateChanged = function(evt) {
	var value = evt.target.getValue();
	if(evt.value != evt.tempOldValue) {
		var isMultiselectObjectConfiguredAndValuesPresent = false;
		var isEditableBasedOnFCConfig = true;
		var isJobStartDateChanged = false;
		var isValidConfig = validateFieldPermission(evt);
		var multiSelectFieldIds = [];
		if (isValidConfig && JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer && JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer!=null) {
			var objFieldList = JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer.getFields();
			for (var idx in objFieldList) {
				if (objFieldList[idx] instanceof RCMMultiSelect) {
					isEditableBasedOnFCConfig = objFieldList[idx].getModel()._isEditableBasedOnFCConfig;
					var selectedValObj= objFieldList[idx].getSelectedValues();
					if(!objFieldList[idx]._readOnly && (selectedValObj.fullySelected || selectedValObj.selectedValues.length > 0)) {
						isMultiselectObjectConfiguredAndValuesPresent = true;
						multiSelectFieldIds.push(objFieldList[idx]);
					} else if (!objFieldList[idx]._readOnly && isEditableBasedOnFCConfig) {
						// if there is no value selected for obj multiselect field,still clear the field so that when 
						//the component is loaded after Job Start date change, the new date considered while picking the data
						objFieldList[idx].clearSelection();
					}
				} 
			}
			if(isMultiselectObjectConfiguredAndValuesPresent) {
				if(!isEditableBasedOnFCConfig) {
				    showAlert();
					retainOldJobStartDateValue(evt);
				}else {
					isJobStartDateChanged = confirmJobStartDateChange(evt, multiSelectFieldIds);
				}
			} else {
				isJobStartDateChanged = true;
			}
			if (isJobStartDateChanged) {
				for (var idx1 in objFieldList) {
					if (objFieldList[idx1] instanceof RCMMultiSelect) {
						objFieldList[idx1].getModel().setEffectiveStartDate(value);
					} else {
						objFieldList[idx1].setEffectiveStartDate(value);
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

function confirmJobStartDateChange(event, multiSelectFieldIds) {
        var dateLabel =  "jobStartDate";
	var clearFields = [];
	for(var index in multiSelectFieldIds) {
	    if(multiSelectFieldIds[index]._customHelpIconConfig)
	      clearFields.push(multiSelectFieldIds[index]._customHelpIconConfig.fieldLabel);
	}
	clearFields.join();
	var confirmMsg = sfMessageFormat.format("Changing the field {0} would delete all the existing values for the field {1}. Do you wish to continue?", dateLabel, clearFields);
	if (confirm(confirmMsg)) {
		if (JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer && JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer!=null) {
			var fieldList = JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer.getFields();
			for (var idx in fieldList) {
				if (fieldList[idx] instanceof RCMMultiSelect) {
					fieldList[idx].clearSelection();
				}
			}
		}
	    return true;
	} else {
		retainOldJobStartDateValue(event);
	}
}

function onEvergreenChange(fieldId){
    var evergreenState = juic.$(fieldId).checked;
    if(!evergreenState && childJobReqs && childJobReqs.getChildJobReqIds().length>0){
	    var errorDialogBox = new RCMDialog("error", "You cannot change an evergreen job requisition to a standard job requisition because the child requisitions are still linked. Unlink the child requisitions and then try changing the evergreen requisition to a standard requisition. If you do not have permission to unlink the child requisition, contact your system administrator.", "Error", "action");
	    errorDialogBox.show();
	    juic.$(fieldId).checked = true;
	}	  
}

function validateFieldPermission(event)	{
	if(false){
		showAlert();
		retainOldJobStartDateValue(event);
		return false;
	} else {
		return true;
	}
}

function showAlert() {
	var errorMsg = "The field Wished assignment start date cannot be changed due to configuration issues. Please contact your System Administrator.";
	var errorDialogBox = new RCMDialog("error", errorMsg, "Alert", "action");
	errorDialogBox.show();
}

var disableNumberOfOpeningValidation=false;
function showNumberOfOpeningsWarning(numberOfOpenings) {
	var numberOpeningsFieldLabel="Number of vacancies"
	var wrngMsg = sfMessageFormat.format("The value for {0} is {1}. Review the value entered to confirm that it is correct per the number of positions assigned to the requisition.\nDo you want to save the requisition with the current value for {2}?", numberOpeningsFieldLabel, numberOfOpenings,numberOpeningsFieldLabel);
	return confirm(wrngMsg);
}

function validateNoOfOpeningForMultiPosition() {
	
	if(!disableNumberOfOpeningValidation){
		var originalNoOpenings=1.0;
		var keyButton=gebi('fb2toolbar_button_field');
		if (keyButton && keyButton.value == 'fb2toolbar_btn_close_without_save') {
		 	 return true; // skip check when close without save
		}
		
		var noOfPositionsSelected=0;
		var isPositionChanged=false;
		if ( JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer && JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer!=null && JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer.getFields ){
			var objFieldList = JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer.getFields();
			for (var idx in objFieldList) {
				if (objFieldList[idx] instanceof RCMMultiSelect) {
					var fieldName = objFieldList[idx].getFieldName();
					if ( fieldName == "std_position_obj" ){
						if (objFieldList[idx].getModel()!=null ){
							noOfPositionsSelected = objFieldList[idx].getModel().getCountOfItemsSelected()
							if(JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer.getFieldsState()[idx]){
								isPositionChanged=true;
							}
						}
						break;
					}
				}
			
			}
		}
		var noOfOpeningsFieldId = "tor_wf_sect_0_fnumberOpenings";
		//Showing warning message is no of positions selected is more than one
		// and either no of openings or positions selected changed after last form submit
		if(noOfPositionsSelected>1 && juic.$(noOfOpeningsFieldId)!=null ){
			var noOfOpeningsValue= juic.$(noOfOpeningsFieldId).value;
			if ( originalNoOpenings != noOfOpeningsValue || isPositionChanged){
				var confirmValue= showNumberOfOpeningsWarning(noOfOpeningsValue);
				disableNumberOfOpeningValidation=confirmValue;
				return confirmValue;
			}	
		}
	
	}
	return true;
}


function retainOldJobStartDateValue(event) {
	var jobStartDateFieldId = "jobStartDate";
	var keyFieldId = "tor_wf_sect_0_fjobStartDate";
	var datePicker = event.target;
	datePicker.setValue(event.tempOldValue == "INVALID" ? "" : event.tempOldValue);
	juic.$(keyFieldId).value = datePicker.getValue();
	var ruleConfigObj = {};
	ruleConfigObj.type= 'date';
	ruleConfigObj.tFldId = jobStartDateFieldId;
	triggerBusinessRules(null, ruleConfigObj);
	return false;
}

var rteUseEditorNameAsId = true;
var RCMJobReqRenderer = {};
var currOperators = {};
var teamOpFieldContainers ={};
var operatorKeyFieldIds = {};

function RCMJobReqPicklistHandler() {
    this._picklistsRequiringDefaultValueReset = [];
}

RCMJobReqPicklistHandler.prototype = (function() {
	return set(new juic.EventTarget(), {
		
		addPicklist : function(picklist) {
			picklist.addEventListener("picklistChanged", this);
		   /*
			* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
			* Listen to the event when a multiselect undergoes selection change from SFCascadingPicklist component.
			*/
			picklist.addEventListener("multiplePicklistsChanged", this);
			
			//Add picklist's field name if has selections and is multiselect that has selectedValues as Object or Array
			var selectedValues = picklist.getSelectedValue();
			if (selectedValues instanceof Object
			    && !(selectedValues instanceof String)) {
			    this._picklistsRequiringDefaultValueReset.push(picklist.getFieldName());
			}
		},

		
		handleEvent : function(evt) {
			switch (evt.type) {
			  case "picklistChanged" :
	            var configObj = {};
	            configObj.type= 'picklist';
	            configObj.tFldId = evt ? evt.fieldName:"";
				var changeContext = evt.changeContext;
				if (!changeContext || (changeContext && !changeContext.fromRules)) {
					triggerBusinessRules(null, configObj );
				}
			  case "multiplePicklistsChanged" :
				var picklistInput = juic.$(evt.target.getFieldName() + "_input");
				if (picklistInput) {
				  //Check if the target is a multiselect or single select. In case of single select, set value of hidden field as it was being set before - through getValue of target
				  if(!evt.target._multiselect){
					  picklistInput.value = evt.target.getValue();
					  //if "adCode" is child of the picklist then unselect all the values in "adCode" if nothing is selected in the parent picklist
					  if(evt.target._childList) {
						var childList = evt.target._childList;
						for(var idx=0; idx < childList.length; idx++) {
						  if(childList[idx] == RCMJobReqRenderer.adCodeFieldId) {
							if(RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists) {
							  for(var pickIdx = 0; pickIdx < RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists.length; pickIdx++) {
								RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists[pickIdx].setOnParentChange(true);
								if(RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists[pickIdx].getFieldName() == RCMJobReqRenderer.adCodeFieldId) {
								  if(RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists[pickIdx]._rcmMultiselect){
								  //setting optionsDialog to null so that it is created again for the new picklist.
								  //this is needed to re-render the select all checkbox properly. Also clearing the selected value
									RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists[pickIdx]._rcmMultiselect._optionsDialog = null;
									RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists[pickIdx]._rcmMultiselect._selectedValue = [];
									RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists[pickIdx]._rcmMultiselect.clearSelection();
								  }
								}
							  }
							}
						  }
						}
					  }
					}else{
						/*
						* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
						* In case of a multiselect do the following
						*	a) set the new values into RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues by calling setMFieldValues
						*	b) set the primary value
						*	c) set the JSON representation of the values read from RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues into respective hidden fields
						*/
						if(evt.newValue){
							//Flush old values from mfield values datastructure for this particular hierarchy only
							var hierarchy = RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[evt.fieldName];
							for(var idx=0;idx<(hierarchy && hierarchy.length);idx++){
								//clear values for hierarchy[idx]
								RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues[hierarchy[idx]] = [];
							}
							this.setMFieldValues(evt.newValue,-1,RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[evt.fieldName],0);
						}
						//Set primary values
						if(evt.primaryValue){
							var primaryValue = evt.primaryValue;
							var primaryValueArray = primaryValue.split(":");
							var fieldHierarchy = RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[evt.fieldName];
							if(primaryValueArray && primaryValueArray.length>0 && fieldHierarchy && fieldHierarchy.length>0){
								var len = fieldHierarchy.length;
								for(var idx=0;idx<=len-1;idx++){
									var currValues = RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues[fieldHierarchy[idx]];
									for(var idx2=0;idx2<(currValues && currValues.length);idx2++){
										if(currValues[idx2].optionId==primaryValueArray[idx]){
											RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues[fieldHierarchy[idx]][idx2].isPrimary = true;
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}

						//Set field values to their hidden inputs (display:none)
						var hierarchy = RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[evt.fieldName];
						var setDefaultValue = false;
						for(var idx=0;idx<(hierarchy && hierarchy.length);idx++){
							var hiddenField = juic.$(hierarchy[idx] + "_input");
							if(hiddenField){
								hiddenField.value = RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues[hierarchy[idx]].length > 0 ? this.getSortedJSONString(RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues[hierarchy[idx]]) : "";
								
								/*
								 * Reset field's default value if picklist just loaded.
								 *
								 * If the multiselect picklist already has values selected when page is loaded, it will go through this flow when page is loading.
								 * It is necessary to reset the default value to the JSON string of objects with properties sorted alphabetically
								 * so that the field's default value and value can be properly compared to see if the field has been modified.
								 * If we don't sort it, the order of the objects' properties are unpredictable.
								 *
								 * --NOTE: Child picklists in the hierarchy are not added to the array. We need the setDefaultValue flag so that the defaultValue
								 *   will be reset for the child picklists as well.
								 */
								var fieldNameIndex = this._picklistsRequiringDefaultValueReset.indexOf(evt.fieldName);
								if (fieldNameIndex > -1 || setDefaultValue) {
								    setDefaultValue = true;
								    if (fieldNameIndex > -1) {
								        this._picklistsRequiringDefaultValueReset.splice(fieldNameIndex, 1);
								    }
								    hiddenField.defaultValue = hiddenField.value;
								}
							}
						}
					}
					//If it's a FADV parent field, dispatch event for refreshing the model in FADV section
					if(RCMJobReqRenderer.fadvAccountMappingConfig !== null) {
							 var parentData = {};
							 parentData.isMultiSelect = (evt.type == "multiplePicklistsChanged") ;
							 if(parentData.isMultiSelect && typeof evt.newValue != "undefined") {
								parentData.newSelectedValues = evt.newValue;
								parentData.primaryValue = evt.primaryValue;
							 }
							 evt.target.dispatch("parentPicklistChanged", {parentData : parentData, onParentChange : evt.onParentChange});
					}
				}
			}
		},
		
        /*
         * Returns a JSON string representation of the array of Objects.
         * The properties are alphabetically sorted in each Object.
         * This is necessary so that form_modified.js can properly compare the
         * JSON strings in the hidden field (default value vs value).
         */		
		getSortedJSONString : function(selectionArray) {
		    var returnArray = [];
		    var selectionArrayLength = selectionArray.length;
		    		    
		    for (var i = 0; i < selectionArrayLength; i ++) {
		        var sortedObject = {};
		        var tempArray = [];
		        var selectionObject = selectionArray[i];
		        
			    for (var key in selectionObject) {
			        if (selectionObject.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
			            tempArray.push(key);
			        }
			    }
			    
			    tempArray.sort();
			    
			    var tempArrayLen = tempArray.length;
			    for (var j = 0; j < tempArrayLen; j ++) {
			        sortedObject[tempArray[j]] = selectionObject[tempArray[j]];
			    }
			    
			    returnArray.push(sortedObject);
		    }
		    
		    return JSON.stringify(returnArray);
		},

		/*
		 * PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
		 * Stores the values of mfields are stored in RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues.
		 */
		setMFieldValues : function(values,parentOptionId,fieldHierarchy,fieldHierarchyIndex){
			var fieldName = fieldHierarchy[fieldHierarchyIndex];
			if (values instanceof Array) {
			   for (var i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
				  RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues[fieldName].push({parentOptionId:parentOptionId,
					  optionId:values[i],isPrimary:false});
			   }
			} else if (values instanceof Object) {
				for(var optionId in values){
					if(!values.hasOwnProperty(optionId)){
						continue;
					}

					if(!RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues[fieldName]){
						RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues[fieldName] = [];
					}

					RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues[fieldName].push({parentOptionId:parentOptionId,optionId:optionId,isPrimary:false});

					if(typeof values[optionId] == 'object'){
						this.setMFieldValues(values[optionId],optionId,fieldHierarchy,fieldHierarchyIndex+1);
					}
				}
			} else {
				   RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues[fieldName].push({parentOptionId:parentOptionId,
				   optionId:values,isPrimary:false});
			 }
		}
  });
})();


RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists = [];


RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistConfigs = [];


RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistManager = null;

RCMJobReqRenderer.adCodeFieldId = "adCode";

RCMJobReqRenderer.fadvAccountMappingConfig = null;

RCMJobReqRenderer.getPicklistManager = function() {
  if(null==RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistManager) {
	RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistManager = new SFCascadingPicklistsManager();
  }
  return RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistManager;
}

RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistChangeHandler = new RCMJobReqPicklistHandler();

/*
* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
* Maps a given field to a picklist id 
*/
RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldToPicklistMapping = {};

/*
* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
* Stores the parent child hierarchy of a top-most parent field 
*/
RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap = {};

/*
* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
*  Stores the parent child hierarchy of a top-most parent picklist
*  Derieved/Constructed once based on fieldToPicklistMapping & fieldHierarchyMap to avoid multiple parsing at runtime
*/
RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistHierarchyMap = {};

/*
* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
* Stores the selected values (optionId, parentOptionId, isPrimary) for a configured mField
*/
RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldValues = {};

/*
* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
* Stores the previously selected values (optionId, parentOptionId, isPrimary) for a configured mField
*/
RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPreselectedValues = {};

/*
* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
* Stores the primary values for a configured top most parent mField
*/
RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPrimaryValues = {};

/*
* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
* Maintains the fieldHierarchyMap by adding the the given fieldName into  fieldHierarchyMap based on the parentPicklistId and childFieldNames
*/
RCMJobReqRenderer.insertIntoFieldHierarchyMap = function(fieldName,parentPicklistId,childFieldNames, isParentMfield){
	if(!parentPicklistId || (parentPicklistId && !isParentMfield)){
		RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[fieldName] = [fieldName];
	}	
	if(childFieldNames && childFieldNames.length>0){
		for(var field in RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap){
			if(RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap.hasOwnProperty(field) && RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[field].contains(fieldName)){
				var noChildren = childFieldNames.length;
				for(var cIdx=0;cIdx<=noChildren-1;cIdx++){
					if(childFieldNames[cIdx]){
						RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[field].push(childFieldNames[cIdx]);
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

/*
* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
* Constructs the picklistHierarchyMap based on fieldHierarchyMap & fieldToPicklistMapping datastructures
*/
RCMJobReqRenderer.constructPickListHierarchy = function(){
	for(var field in RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap){
		if(RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap.hasOwnProperty(field) && RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldToPicklistMapping[field]){
			var currPicklists = [];
			var childrenFields = RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[field];
			for(var idx=0;idx<=(childrenFields && childrenFields.length-1);idx++){
				currPicklists.push(RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldToPicklistMapping[childrenFields[idx]]);
			}
			RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistHierarchyMap[field+"_"+RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldToPicklistMapping[field]]=currPicklists;
		}
	}
}



	  /*
	  * PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
	  * isMultiselect attribute added. Passed from FBJobReqRenderer.java 'drawPicklistField' method.
	  * isMultiselect indicates if the picklist is configured as a multiselect in the template.
	  */
RCMJobReqRenderer.addNewPicklist = function (fieldName, picklistId, selectedValue, childPicklistIds, toolTipText, parentPicklistId, isMultiselect, isRequired, isInvalid, labelForId, fieldLabel) {

	   /*
		* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
		* Set the previously selected values into mFieldPreselectedValues data structure
		*/
		if(isMultiselect && selectedValue){
			RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPreselectedValues[fieldName] = JSON.parse(selectedValue);
		}
		var isHierarchicalMode = isMultiselect;
		var isHasPrimary = isMultiselect;
		var isParentMfield = true;

		if (fieldName === RCMJobReqRenderer.adCodeFieldId) {
			isHierarchicalMode = isHasPrimary =false;
			if(parentPicklistId) {
			  isParentMfield = RCMJobReqRenderer.isParentMfield();
			}
		}

	   var picklistConfig = {
					fieldName         : fieldName,
					picklistId        : picklistId,
					childPicklistIds  : childPicklistIds,
					parentPicklistId  : parentPicklistId,
					validationMsg     : false,
					selectedValue     : selectedValue,
					toolTipText       : toolTipText,
					multiselect       : isMultiselect,
					hierarchicalMode  : isHierarchicalMode,
					hasPrimary        : isHasPrimary,
					required          : isRequired,
					invalid           : isInvalid,
					labelForId        : labelForId,
					label             : fieldLabel
				   };

		/*
		* PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
		* Construct the fieldToPicklistMapping & fieldHierarchyMap
		*/
	   if(isMultiselect){
			//populate the fieldToPicklistMapping
			RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldToPicklistMapping[fieldName] =picklistId;
			
			RCMJobReqRenderer.insertIntoFieldHierarchyMap(fieldName,parentPicklistId,childPicklistIds,isParentMfield);
	   }
	   
	   /*
		In case of multiSelects, preserve only the top most parent's picklist config
		In case of Non Hierarchical multi-select fields like ""adCode" if the parent is an mField
		then preserve only the top field, else show the multiselect field also
	   */
	   if((!isMultiselect) || ((isMultiselect && !parentPicklistId) || !isParentMfield)){
		   RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistConfigs.push(picklistConfig);
	   }
};

RCMJobReqRenderer.isParentMfield = function() {
  var isParentMfield = false
  return isParentMfield;
};

/*
 * PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
 * Construct the mFieldPreselectedValues
 */
RCMJobReqRenderer.constructMfieldSelectedValue = function (){
	for(var field in RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap){
		if(!RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap.hasOwnProperty(field)){
			continue;
		}

		//Create single list of selected values for the hierarchy of a given parentfield - field
		var selectedValues = [];
		if(RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[field]){
			var len = RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[field].length;

			for(var idx=0;idx<=len-1;idx++){
				var childArray = RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPreselectedValues[RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[field][idx]];
				if(childArray){
					selectedValues = selectedValues.concat(childArray);
					RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPreselectedValues[RCMJobReqRenderer.fieldHierarchyMap[field][idx]] = null;
				}
			}
		}

        //construct the selected value for the field
        if(selectedValues && selectedValues.length>0){
            var fieldPicklistConfig;
            var length = RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistConfigs.length;
            for (var configIdx = 0; configIdx< length; configIdx++) {
                if (RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistConfigs[configIdx].fieldName === field) {
                        fieldPicklistConfig = RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistConfigs[configIdx];
                        break;
                }
            }
            var preselectedValue = fieldPicklistConfig && fieldPicklistConfig.hierarchicalMode ? {} : [];
            var lookup = {};
            RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPreselectedValues[field] = preselectedValue;
            for(var idx=0;idx<=selectedValues.length-1;idx++){
                var currentValue = selectedValues[idx];
                if(selectedValues[idx].isPrimary){
                    if(!RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPrimaryValues[field]){
                        RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPrimaryValues[field] = [];
                    }
                    RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPrimaryValues[field].push(selectedValues[idx].optionId);
                }
                if (fieldPicklistConfig && fieldPicklistConfig.hierarchicalMode) {
                    RCMJobReqRenderer._addValueToHierarchy(preselectedValue,
                        currentValue.optionId, currentValue.parentOptionId, lookup);
                } else {
                    RCMJobReqRenderer._addValueToMultiselect(preselectedValue,
                        currentValue.optionId, currentValue.parentOptionId);
                }
            }
        }

	}
};

/*
 * PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
 * Gets the primary value based on the mFieldPrimaryValues data structure for a given field
 */
RCMJobReqRenderer.getPrimaryValue = function(fieldName){
	var primaryValueArray = RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPrimaryValues[fieldName];
	var primaryValue = "";
	if(primaryValueArray && primaryValueArray.length>0){
		for(var idx=0;idx<(primaryValueArray.length);idx++){
			if(idx!=0){
				primaryValue += ":";
			}
			
			primaryValue += primaryValueArray[idx];
		}
	}
	
	return primaryValue;
};

/**
* This function is called multiple times with a flat list of selected values and
* will incrementally build the heirarchy by adding to the input object.
*
* @param {Object} object The selected value or root of the heirarchy
* @param {Integer} optionId The selected option id (or child)
* @param {Integer} parentOptionId The parent of the given optionId or -1
* @param {Object} lookup A lookup table of all parentOptionIds
*/
RCMJobReqRenderer._addValueToHierarchy = function(object,optionId,parentOptionId,lookup){
    lookup[optionId] = parentOptionId;
    //Find correct hierarchy using lookup.
    var currentOptionId = optionId;
    var stack = [];
    while(lookup[currentOptionId] && lookup[currentOptionId] != -1) { //Store the reverse hierarchy (from current node to root) in the stack
        stack.push(lookup[currentOptionId]);
        currentOptionId = lookup[currentOptionId];
    }
    
    var currentObject = object;
    while(stack.length > 1){ // Get the node which has the parent object of the current node from the hierarchy
        currentObject = currentObject[stack.pop()];
    }
    
    if(currentObject[parentOptionId]) {
        if(typeof currentObject[parentOptionId] == "boolean"){
            currentObject[parentOptionId] = {};
        }
        currentObject[parentOptionId][optionId] = true; 
    } else {
        currentObject[optionId] = true; //For the selected elements in the root node
    } 
};

RCMJobReqRenderer._addValueToMultiselect = function(selected,optionId,parentOptionId) {
	if(parentOptionId == -1) {
		selected.push(optionId);
	}
};


RCMJobReqRenderer.renderJobReqPicklists = function renderJobReqPicklists() {
  RCMJobReqRenderer.constructPickListHierarchy();
  RCMJobReqRenderer.constructMfieldSelectedValue();
  

  for (var idxConfig=0,lenOfItems = RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistConfigs.length; idxConfig < lenOfItems; idxConfig++) {
	var picklistConfig = RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistConfigs[idxConfig];
	 /*
	 * PAE-367: Multiselect fields in job req forms
	 * set the multiselect related config items into picklist config which is passed to SFCascadingPicklist
	 */
	if(picklistConfig && picklistConfig.multiselect){
		picklistConfig.picklistHierarchy = RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistHierarchyMap[picklistConfig.fieldName+"_"+picklistConfig.picklistId];
		picklistConfig.selectedValue = RCMJobReqRenderer.mFieldPreselectedValues[picklistConfig.fieldName];
		picklistConfig.primaryValue = RCMJobReqRenderer.getPrimaryValue(picklistConfig.fieldName);
	}
	picklistConfig["picklistMgr"] = RCMJobReqRenderer.getPicklistManager();
	picklistConfig.paginatedPicklist = true; // to render the paginated picklists UI
	//if it is the non-hierarchical multi-select field adCode with a non mfield parent and parent has a selected value then
	//in that case creating the default option list
	if(picklistConfig.fieldName === RCMJobReqRenderer.adCodeFieldId && picklistConfig.parentPicklistId) {
	  if(!RCMJobReqRenderer.isParentMfield()) {
		var parentSelectedVal = RCMJobReqRenderer.getParentPicklistSelectedValue();
		if(parentSelectedVal != "") {
		  if(picklistConfig.picklist && picklistConfig.picklist.picklistObjects) {
			var opList = RCMJobReqRenderer.getOptionList(picklistConfig.picklist.picklistObjects, parentSelectedVal);
			if(opList.length > 1) {
			  picklistConfig.defaultOptionList = opList;
			}
		  }
		}
	  }
	}
	var picklistComponent = new SFCascadingPicklist(picklistConfig);


	if (picklistConfig.fieldName === RCMJobReqRenderer.adCodeFieldId) {
		if (picklistComponent._rcmMultiselect){
			picklistComponent._rcmMultiselect._allSelectedLabel = MSGS.COMMON_All;
		}
	}
	if(RCMJobReqRenderer.fadvAccountMappingConfig !== null) {
		var fadvParentFieldId = RCMJobReqRenderer.fadvAccountMappingConfig.parentFieldId;
		if (picklistConfig.fieldName === fadvParentFieldId) {
			RCMJobReqRenderer.fadvAccountMappingConfig.picklistComponent = picklistComponent;
		 }
	}
	RCMJobReqRenderer.picklistChangeHandler.addPicklist(picklistComponent);
	RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists.push(picklistComponent);
	picklistComponent.render(picklistComponent.getFieldName());
  }
};

RCMJobReqRenderer.getParentPicklistSelectedValue = function() {
  var parentSelectedVal = "";
  return parentSelectedVal;
};

RCMJobReqRenderer.getOptionList = function(picklist, parentSelectedVal) {
  var opList = [{label:"No Selection", value:""}];
  var pickLen = picklist.length;
  for(var idx = 0; idx < pickLen; idx++) {
	if(typeof picklist[idx].parentOptionId != "undefined"){
	  if(picklist[idx].parentOptionId == parentSelectedVal) {
		opList.push(picklist[idx])
	  }
	}
  }
  
  return opList;
};

RCMJobReqRenderer.getPicklistByFieldName = function getPicklistByFieldName(fieldName) {
  for (var idx=0; idx < RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists.length; idx++) {
	var picklist = RCMJobReqRenderer.picklists[idx];
	if (picklist.getFieldName() == fieldName) {
	  return picklist;
	}
  }
}

	
function confirmCloseReq(event){
	var confirmMsg = '';
	if (event != null && event.srcElement != null && event.srcElement.className.indexOf('cancelJobRequisition') > -1) {
		confirmMsg += "You are about to cancel this Job Event/Requisition ";
		if (confirm(confirmMsg)) {
			var closeReq = document.getElementById('tor_wf_sect_0_closeReq');
			if (closeReq) {
				closeReq.value = "true";
			}
			document.forms[0].submit();
		} else {
			return false;
		}
	} else {
		if (templateObjectValidator.validateAllFields()) {
			var oldStatus = 'Job Requisition Creation';
			var statusPicklist = RCMJobReqRenderer.getPicklistByFieldName('status');
			var closeStatus = statusPicklist ? statusPicklist.getLabelByValue(statusPicklist.getValue()) : null;
			if(false) {
			        var confirmMsg = ''+'\n';
			}
			
				confirmMsg += "You are closing the job requisition ";
			
			if(closeStatus) {
				confirmMsg += "with a status of "+closeStatus;
			} else if (oldStatus && oldStatus!="") {
				confirmMsg += "with a status of "+oldStatus;
			}
			if(false) {
            	confirmMsg += ". Closing the job requisition will also move the pending offers to the Cancelled status.";
            }
			if(confirm(confirmMsg)) {
				var closeReq = document.getElementById('tor_wf_sect_0_closeReq');
				if(closeReq) {
					closeReq.value = "true";
				}
                
		  	        if(juic.$("recruiting_ns")){
		  			    setField("recruiting_ns","jobreqDetail");
				    }
   			    				
				document.forms[0].submit();
			} else {
				return false;
			}
		}
	}
  	return false;
}

function confirmCloseReqNoSubmit(){
  if(templateObjectValidator.validateAllFields()){
  var oldStatus = 'Job Requisition Creation';
  var statusPicklist = RCMJobReqRenderer.getPicklistByFieldName('status');
  var closeStatus = statusPicklist ? statusPicklist.getLabelByValue(statusPicklist.getValue()) : null;
  
  
  var confirmMsg = "You are closing the job requisition ";
  
  if(closeStatus){
	confirmMsg += "with a status of "+closeStatus;
  } else if (oldStatus && oldStatus!=""){
	confirmMsg += "with a status of "+oldStatus;
  }
  if(false){
    confirmMsg += ". Closing the job requisition will also move the pending offers to the Cancelled status.";
  }
  if(confirm(confirmMsg)){
	var closeReq = document.getElementById('tor_wf_sect_0_closeReq');
	if(closeReq){
	  closeReq.value = "true";
	}
	return true;

  } else {
	return false;
  }
  }
}

function confirmReopenReq(){
  var reOpenEnabled = true ? 'true' : null; 
  if(!reOpenEnabled){
  alert('Requisition cannot be reopened as there are no open positions remaining for this requisition');
  return false;
  }
  var oldStatus = 'Job Requisition Creation';
  var statusPicklist = RCMJobReqRenderer.getPicklistByFieldName('status');
  var closeStatus = statusPicklist ? statusPicklist.getLabelByValue(statusPicklist.getValue()) : null;
 
  var confirmMsg = "You are about to reopen this Job Req ";
  
  if(closeStatus){
	confirmMsg += "with a status of "+closeStatus;
  } else if (oldStatus && oldStatus!=""){
	confirmMsg += "with a status of "+oldStatus;
  }
  if(confirm(confirmMsg)){
	var reopenReq = document.getElementById('tor_wf_sect_0_reopenReq');
	if(reopenReq){
	  reopenReq.value = "true";
	}
  
    if(juic.$("recruiting_ns")){
      setField("recruiting_ns","jobreqDetail");
    }
  
	document.forms[0].submit();
  } else {
	return false;
  }  
  return true;
}

  }
  if(confirm(confirmMsg)){
	var reopenReq = document.getElementById('tor_wf_sect_0_reopenReq');

	}

}

function isValidClosedStatusSelected(selectedClosedStatus){
    var allClosedStatus = '';
    var allClosedStatusArray = allClosedStatus.split(","); 
    for(i = 0; i < allClosedStatusArray.length; i++){
      if(allClosedStatusArray[i] == selectedClosedStatus){
       return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
}

function setErrorOnObjFields() {
	var objFields = JobReqObjectTypeFieldRenderer.getFields();
	for (var idx in objFields) {
		if (objFields[idx].checkForErrors()) {
			juic.$(objFields[idx]._objField.id).classList.add("invalidInput");
		} else {
			juic.$(objFields[idx]._objField.id).classList.remove("invalidInput");
		}
	}
}

function setFocusFirstErrorField() {
	var reInFocusFieldId = [];
	var allFieldList = templateObjectValidator.validator.fieldList;
	for (var i=0 ; i< allFieldList.length ; ++i) {
		if (juic.$(allFieldList[i].id)) {
			var err = allFieldList[i].validate();
			if (err) {
				reInFocusFieldId.push(allFieldList[i].id);

				if(juic.$(allFieldList[i].id).getAttribute('type') === "hidden" || juic.$(allFieldList[i].id).getAttribute('style') === "display:none;") {
					var errorElem = juic.$(allFieldList[i].id).previousElementSibling || juic.$(allFieldList[i].id).parentElement.previousElementSibling;
					errorElem.tagName === "DIV" ? errorElem.classList.add("invalidInput") : errorElem.querySelector("div").classList.add("invalidInput");
				}
			} else {
				if(juic.$(allFieldList[i].id).getAttribute('type') === "hidden" || juic.$(allFieldList[i].id).getAttribute('style') === "display:none;") {
					var errorElem = juic.$(allFieldList[i].id).previousElementSibling || juic.$(allFieldList[i].id).parentElement.previousElementSibling;
					errorElem.tagName === "DIV" ? errorElem.classList.remove("invalidInput") : errorElem.querySelector("div").classList.remove("invalidInput");
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if(reInFocusFieldId.length > 0) {
		SFDom.setFocus(reInFocusFieldId[0]);
	}
}

  function saveForm(){
    if ( validateNoOfOpeningForMultiPosition() && templateObjectValidator.validateAllFields()) {
	  var oldStatus = 'Job Requisition Creation';
	  var statusPicklist = RCMJobReqRenderer.getPicklistByFieldName('status');
	  var closeStatus = statusPicklist ? statusPicklist.getLabelByValue(statusPicklist.getValue()) : null;
	  var isClosedButtonEnabled = false;
	  if(isClosedButtonEnabled && closeStatus && isValidClosedStatusSelected(closeStatus))
	  {
	    var confirmMsg = ''+'\n';
	   

		confirmMsg += "You are closing the job requisition ";
		
		if(closeStatus){
		  confirmMsg += "with a status of "+closeStatus;
		} else if (oldStatus && oldStatus!=""){
		  confirmMsg += "with a status of "+oldStatus;
		}
		if(false){
            confirmMsg += ". Closing the job requisition will also move the pending offers to the Cancelled status.";
        }
		if(!confirm(confirmMsg))
		return false;
	  }
	  if ( document.getElementById("recruiting_ns")){
		setField("recruiting_ns", "jobreqDetail");
	  }
	  loadWindow();
	  window.onbeforeunload=null;
	  return true;
	} else {
	  setFocusFirstErrorField();
	  setErrorOnObjFields();
	  return false;
	}
  }

    return function () {
        if(validateNoOfOpeningForMultiPosition())
        	return checkRTEComment.call();
        else
        	return false;
    };
}(window.checkRTEComment);

	rcmContentRuleModel.locale = selectedLang.options[selectedLang.selectedIndex].value ;
  } else {
	rcmContentRuleModel.locale = defaultLang.value ;
  }

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'department', 'tor_wf_sect_0_fdepartment');

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'location', 'tor_wf_sect_0_flocation');

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'filter1', 'tor_wf_sect_0_ffilter1');

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'filter2', 'tor_wf_sect_0_ffilter2');

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'filter3', 'tor_wf_sect_0_ffilter3');

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'filter4', 'tor_wf_sect_0_ffilter4');

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'filter5', 'tor_wf_sect_0_ffilter5');

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'filter6', 'tor_wf_sect_0_ffilter6');

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'filter7', 'tor_wf_sect_0_ffilter7');

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'filter8', 'tor_wf_sect_0_ffilter8');

		populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, 'filter9', 'tor_wf_sect_0_ffilter9');

  new RCMInfoRadioButton(rcmContentRuleModel, document.activeElement);
}

function populateRCMDescContentRule(rcmContentRuleModel, filterId, filterFieldIdOrName) {
	var filterObj = document.getElementById(filterFieldIdOrName);
	if(filterObj) {
		rcmContentRuleModel[filterId] = filterObj.value;
	} else {
		filterObj = document.getElementsByName(filterFieldIdOrName);
		if (filterObj && filterObj.length > 0) {
			rcmContentRuleModel[filterId] = filterObj[0].value;
		}
	}
}



  function populateHeaderFooter(resultArray) {
  var selectedId;
  var rcmContentRuleModel;
  var radioButtonArray = document.getElementsByName("ruleId");
  if(radioButtonArray && radioButtonArray.length) {
	for(i = 0; i < radioButtonArray.length; i++){
	  if(radioButtonArray[i].checked){
		selectedId = radioButtonArray[i].value;
		break;
	  }
	}
  } else {
	if(radioButtonArray && radioButtonArray.checked){
	  selectedId = radioButtonArray.value;
	}
  }

  for(j = 0; j < resultArray.length; j++){
	if(resultArray[j].contentRuleId == selectedId) {
	  rcmContentRuleModel = resultArray[j];
	  gebi('selectedRuleName').value=rcmContentRuleModel.contentRuleName;
	  break;
	}
  }
  if(rcmContentRuleModel) {

}
}

  }


function loadStateProvinceList(countryList){

  var countryCode = countryList.options[countryList.selectedIndex] ? countryList.options[countryList.selectedIndex].value : null;
  if(countryCode != null){
	var stateSelectList = document.getElementById('');
	if (stateSelectList) {
	  stateSelectList.options.length = 0;
	  stateSelectList.options[0] = new Option('No Selection', '');
	  var url = '/rcmjsup?m=searchProvincesByCountry&country=' + countryCode;
	  url += "&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey;
	  if (submitAjaxQuery(url)) {
		if (queried_items > 0) {
		  for(var i = 0; i < items.length; i++){
			var state = items[i];
			stateSelectList.options[stateSelectList.options.length] = new Option(state, state);
		  }
		}
	  }
	}
  }
}

			}


function LanguagePopup() {
  this.register();
  this._init();
}

(function() {
  juic.extend(LanguagePopup, juic.Component, {	
    _init: function() {
      this._callout = '';
      this._anchorId = '';
    },

    show: function(anchorId) {
      this._anchorId = anchorId;
      if (!this._callout) {
        this._callout = new SFCalloutPopup({
          title: "Select Job languages",
          content: new languageUpdatePopup(),
          clickOutsideClosesPopup: true,
          closeOnMouseout: false,
          shouldSetAriaDescribedBy: false,
          refocusRef: anchorId,
          originOptions: { direction:'right', pointerOffset: 'middle' }
        });
      }
      this._callout.show(anchorId);
      juic.$(anchorId).removeAttribute('aria-describedby');
      juic.$(this._callout.getReferenceId()).removeAttribute('aria-labelledby');
      juic.$(this._callout.getReferenceId()).classList.add('language-popup');
      juic.$(this._callout.getReferenceId() + 'content').classList.remove('globalPortletBody');
    },

    hide: function() {
      if (this._callout) {
        this._callout.hide();
        if (this._anchorId) {
          juic.$(this._anchorId).removeAttribute('aria-describedby');
        }
      }
    }
});
})();
			
var languagePopup = new LanguagePopup();

	  var supportedLang = [];
var languages=[{title:"English (United Kingdom)",checked:true,disabled:true,value:"en_GB"},{title:"French (France)",checked:false,disabled:false,value:"fr_FR"}];
		function languageUpdatePopup(refocusId) {
			this.register();
			var hasFDStyles = Util.isFioriFDEnabled();
			this._closeButton = new SFCommandButton("OK", !hasFDStyles, true, false, { baseButtonWrapperClass: "language-popup-close-btn" });
			this._closeButton.setActionCommand("close");
			this._closeButton.addEventListener("action", this);
			this._changed = false;

			if(refocusId)
			  this._refocusId = refocusId;
		}

		languageUpdatePopup.prototype = (function() {
			return set(new Component(), {
				renderHtml: function(h) {
					h.push("<div id=\"", this.id ,"\" class=\"jobLanguageList\" style=\"width:250px;max-height:500px;\">Select the language(s) in which you will accept applications for this job requisition:",
							"<ul aria-label=\"Select Job languages\" role=\"group\" class=\"ckrbList\">");
					var default_lang = 'en_GB';

					for (var idx = 0,len=languages.length;idx < len;idx++) {
						var _isDefault = false;
						if (default_lang == languages[idx].value){
							_isDefault = true;
						}
						h.push("<li><input  class=\"", Util.generateFDClasses("checkbox"), "\"  id=\"CB",idx,"\" onclick=\"", this.fireCode('_valueChanged') ,"\" value=\"",
								languages[idx].value,"\" type=\"checkbox\" ",(languages[idx].checked ? "checked" : ""),((languages[idx].disabled || _isDefault ) ? " disabled=\"true\"" : "")," />",
								"<label class=\"", Util.generateFDClasses("checkbox__label"), "\" for=\"CB",idx,"\">",
								"<span class=\"", Util.generateFDClasses("checkbox__text"), "\">",
									_isDefault ? (languages[idx].title + " (Default)") : languages[idx].title, languages[idx].disabled ? ("(Current)") : "",
							    "</span>",
								"</label></li>");
					}
					h.push("</ul>");
					this._closeButton.renderHtml(h);
					h.push("</div>");

					var id = this.id;
					var elementInterval = window.setInterval(function(){
					  var $el = $(id) || null;

					  if($el){
					    try {
                            $el.querySelectorAll('input:not([disabled])')[0].focus();
                            clearInterval(elementInterval);
                        } catch (e) {}
					  }
					},100);
				},
				_valueChanged: function() {
				   this._changed = true;
				},
				handleEvent: function(evt) {
					switch(evt.type) {
						case "action":
							if (evt.actionCommand === "close") {
								this._closeButton.setEnabled(false);
							 if (this._changed) {

                                /* Update the selected languages without the need to submit the form */
                                 supportedLang = []; //I need to reset this array as it will be rebuilt always when adding/removing languages
                                 var default_lang = 'en_GB';
                                 supportedLang.push(default_lang);
                                 var selectedLanguagesString = 'English (United Kingdom)';
								 for (var idx = 0,len=languages.length;idx<len;idx++) {
								   var cb = gebi('CB'+idx);
								   languages[idx].checked = cb.checked;

									if (cb.checked && cb.value != default_lang) {
									   supportedLang.push(cb.value);
									   selectedLanguagesString += (selectedLanguagesString.length > 0) ? "," + languages[idx].title : languages[idx].title;
									}

								 }
								 gebi('selectedSupportedLang').value = supportedLang.join(',');
								 if(juic.$("recruiting_ns")){
								   setField("recruiting_ns","jobreqDetail");
								 }
		
								 if (languagePopup._anchorId) {
									var refocusId = languagePopup._anchorId;
									localStorage.setItem("refocusRef", refocusId);
								 }

								 this.unregister();
								 document.forms[0].submit();

								 var selectedLanguagesDivBox = juic.$("jobLanguageTextValues");
								 if (selectedLanguagesDivBox) {
								 	selectedLanguagesDivBox.innerHTML = "";
								 	selectedLanguagesDivBox.innerHTML = selectedLanguagesString;
								 }

							 }

							 languagePopup.hide();
							 this._closeButton.setEnabled(true);

							}
					}
				}
			});
		})();

 window.onload = function () {
	var focusOnUpdateBtn = localStorage.getItem('refocusRef');
	if (focusOnUpdateBtn) {
		localStorage.removeItem('refocusRef');
		var updateBtnEl = juic.$(focusOnUpdateBtn);
		updateBtnEl && updateBtnEl.focus();
	}
}

 function selectLangChange()
 {
   gebi('changeSelectedLang').value = 'changeSelectedLang';   

		if(juic.$("recruiting_ns")){
		  setField("recruiting_ns","jobreqDetail");
		}
   
   window.onbeforeunload=null; 
   document.forms[0].submit();
 }

 }
