  function enableTab(tabId) {
    invi(tabId+'LinkSelected', 1, 'inline');
    invi(tabId+'Link', 0);
    invi(tabId+'Box',1);
    var selectedEl = juic.$(tabId+'Tab');
    selectedEl.className='selected';
    var searchTab = juic.$("searchTab");
    var browseTab = juic.$("browseTab");
    var createTab = juic.$("createTab");
    if(searchTab){
        searchTab.setAttribute("aria-selected","false");
    }
    if(browseTab){
        browseTab.setAttribute("aria-selected","false");
    }
    if(createTab){
        createTab.setAttribute("aria-selected","false");
    }
    selectedEl.setAttribute("aria-selected","true");
    document.getElementById('addQuest2Req_selectedTab').value=tabId;
  }

  function disableTab(tabId) {
    invi(tabId+'LinkSelected',0);
    invi(tabId+'Link',1,'inline');
    invi(tabId+'Box',0);
    document.getElementById(tabId+'Tab').className='';
  }

function addQuestion(qid,varChecked, eid) {
	  /* Modified to append the question id to the hidden variable only if its checked- earlier it
	  was appending just on click */
	     var addBttonFromSearch = document.getElementsByName('add_q_from_search')[0];
         var addBttonFrombrowse = document.getElementsByName('add_q_from_browse')[0];
	  	 elem = document.getElementById(eid);
	       var temp = elem.value;
	       qid = qid.substring(7, qid.length);
	        if(varChecked == true){
	     		temp = temp+''+qid+',';
	       	elem.value = temp;
	        if((eid == "selected_in_search" || eid == "selected_in_local") && addBttonFromSearch){
                addBttonFromSearch.removeAttribute("disabled");
            }
            if((eid == "selected_in_browse" || eid == "selected_in_local") && addBttonFrombrowse){
                addBttonFrombrowse.removeAttribute("disabled");
            }
	       }else{
	  // To remove the qid if it was unselected
	  	    var tempArray = temp.split(",");
	  	    var newTemp = '';
	          for(i=0;i<tempArray.length;i++){
	               if(tempArray[i] != qid )
	               {
	                 newTemp = newTemp+''+tempArray[i]+',';
	          }
	       }
	          elem.value = newTemp;
	          var reg=/\d/;
              if(!reg.test(elem.value)){
                if((eid == "selected_in_search" || eid == "selected_in_local") && addBttonFromSearch){
                    addBttonFromSearch.setAttribute('disabled','false');
                }
                if((eid == "selected_in_browse" || eid == "selected_in_local") && addBttonFrombrowse){
                    addBttonFrombrowse.setAttribute('disabled','false');
                }
              }
	        }
	  }

  var numOfSelected = 0;

  function toggleRemove(id) {
    elem = document.getElementById(id);
    // alert('Is this checkbox checked? '+elem.checked);
    if (elem.checked) {
      numOfSelected = numOfSelected +1;
    } else {
      numOfSelected = numOfSelected -1;
    }
    // alert('Num of selected: '+numOfSelected);
    if ( numOfSelected > 0)
      document.getElementById('delete_question').disabled = false;
    else
      document.getElementById('delete_question').disabled = true;
  }

  function expandNode(id) {
    invi(id, 1);
    invi('close_' + id, 1);
    invi('close_' + id + '_link', 1, 'inline');
    invi('open_' + id , 0);
    invi('open_' + id + '_link', 0, 'inline');
  }

  function collapseNode(id) {
    invi(id, 0);
    invi('close_' + id, 0);
    invi('close_' + id + '_link', 0, 'inline');
    invi('open_' + id, 1);
    invi('open_' + id + '_link', 1, 'inline');
  }

  /**
   *
   * @param String sDomElementId - The DOM Id of the element to change the aria-hidden attribute value
   * @param String sAriaValue - The new value of the aria-hidden attribute
   */
  function changeAriaHiddenAttribute(sDomElementId, sAriaValue) {
      var domElement = document.getElementById(sDomElementId);
      domElement.setAttribute("aria-hidden", sAriaValue);
  }


  function changeCheckboxQuestionSpanTextJaws(domSpanElem, isPublic){
        return function(){
            if (this.checked){
                RCMElementsUtil.message.talk('Checked');
                domSpanElem.innerText = 'Tickbox';
            } else {
                RCMElementsUtil.message.talk('Unticked');
                domSpanElem.innerText = 'Tickbox not ticked';
            };

            if (isPublic){
                addQuestion(this.id, this.checked, 'selected_in_browse');
            } else {
                addQuestion(this.id, this.checked, 'selected_in_local');
            }
        };
  }


  function requestContent(id) {
    var contentElem = document.getElementById(id + "_val");
    var contentId = contentElem.value;
    parentElem = document.getElementById(id);
    var libName = "";
    var catName = "";
    if (juic.$(id + "_lib")) {
        libName = juic.$(id + "_lib").value;
    }
    if (juic.$(id + "_cat")) {
        catName = juic.$(id + "_cat").value;
    }
    // if (parentElem.childNodes.length > 0) {
    //  alert('parent already has element '+parentElem.childNodes.length);
    //  return;
    // }
    parentElem.innerHTML = "";
    var url = "/rcmjsup?m=jobReqGetQuestoins";
  	//Added locale parameter in the request to get the questions based
    // on the user selected locale
    url += "&contentId=" + encodeURIComponent(contentId) + "&libName=" + encodeURIComponent(libName) + "&catName=" + encodeURIComponent(catName) +"&locale="+encodeURIComponent(rcmQuestionLanguages.getSelectedLanguage());
    url += "&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey;
    addPageAction(RecruitingActionType.GET_JOBREQ_QUESTIONS);
    if (submitAjaxQuestionQuery(url)) {
      if (queried_items > 0) {
        parentElem = document.getElementById(id);
        for (var i=0; i< items.length; i++) {
            var question = items[i];

            // Added this if condition to filtering the top level
            // questions displaying on the UI

              if(question.questionParentId <0){
            	divElem = document.createElement("div");
                divElem.className = "browseLineItem clear_all globalFloatLeft";
                var labelId = "btabpub" + question.questionId + "label";
                labelSpanElem = document.createElement("span");
                labelSpanElem.className = "sr-only";
                labelSpanElem.innerText = 'Tickbox not ticked';

                var checkboxElem = document.createElement("input");
                checkboxElem.setAttribute("type", "checkbox");
                checkboxElem.setAttribute("name", "question_"+question.questionId);
                checkboxElem.setAttribute("aria-labelledby", labelId);
                checkboxElem.setAttribute("role","treeitem");
                checkboxElem.className = "globalFloatLeft " + Util.generateFDClasses("checkbox");
                checkboxElem.onclick = changeCheckboxQuestionSpanTextJaws(labelSpanElem, question.isPublic);
                checkboxElem.onkeydown = RCMAccessibilityTools.keyDownHandlerTree;

            	if (question.isPublic) {
                    checkboxElem.setAttribute("id",  "btabpub"+question.questionId);
                } else {
                    checkboxElem.setAttribute("id", "btabloc"+question.questionId);
                }

                divElem.appendChild(checkboxElem);

                    spanElem = document.createElement("label");
                    spanElem.id = labelId;
                    spanElem.setAttribute("role","presentation");
                    spanElem.setAttribute("for", (question.isPublic ? 'btabpub' : 'btabloc') + question.questionId);
                    spanElem.className = "globalFloatLeft " + Util.generateFDClasses("checkbox__label");

                    var spanLabelText = document.createElement("span");
                    spanLabelText.innerText = question.questionName;
                    spanLabelText.textContent = question.questionName;
                    spanLabelText.className = Util.generateFDClasses("checkbox__text");

                  spanElem.appendChild(spanLabelText);
                  spanElem.appendChild(labelSpanElem);

                  divElem.appendChild(spanElem);
              }
              // Added this if condition to show the Cascade Image only
              // if the top level question has sub questions
                if(question.subQuestionsAvailable == "true"){
            	var space = document.createElement("span");
            	space.className = "smallIconPadding bottompad5 cascadeIconSpan sapIcon globalFloatLeft";
                space.innerHTML ='&#xe0d1;';
            	space.title = "Cascaded Question";
            	spanElem.appendChild(space);
              }
              parentElem.appendChild(divElem);
        } //end of for loop
      } //end if (queried_items > 0)
    } // end if (submitAjaxQuestionQuery(url))
  }

 function submitAjaxQuestionQuery(url) {
  prepareAjaxRequest();
  if (req) {
    try {
      req.open("GET", url, false);
      req.send(null);

      if (req.status != 200) {
        alert("Status "+req.status);
        error_text = req.statusText;
        return false;
      }
      if (req.getResponseHeader("Content-Type").indexOf("text/plain") == -1) {
        error_text = "Your session has ended.";
        alert(error_text);
        return false;
      }

      var responseObject = JSON.parse(req.responseText);
      queried_items = responseObject.queried_items;
      total_items = responseObject.total_items;
      items = responseObject.items;
    } catch (e) {
      error_text = e.message;
      return false;
    }
  }
  return true;
 }

 function confirmDeleteDesc(deleteMenu, blockId, addLink, hideLink, actionMenu) {
   input_entry = confirm('Are you sure you want to delete the description for this question?');
   if (input_entry == true) {
      deleteMenu.className = this.className.replace('over', '');
      invi(deleteMenu.id,0);
      invi(blockId,0);
      showHideLayers(addLink, hideLink);
      invi(actionMenu, 0);
      alert('The description has been deleted.');
    }
 }

 function findParent(n,name) {
  while (n.tagName != name) { n = n.parentNode; }
  return n;
}

 function confirmDeleteQuestion(deleteMenu, actionMenu, questionId,fmQuestionId,nestCount) {
   quesIndex=questionId;
   input_entry = confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this question?');
   if (input_entry == true) {
     deleteMenu.className = deleteMenu.className.replace('over', '');
     invi(actionMenu, 0);
     qlist = document.getElementById('addQuest2Req_deleted_quest').value;
     tr = findParent(deleteMenu, "TR");
     tBody=  findParent(deleteMenu, "TBODY");
     if (tr) {
       var p = tr.parentNode;
       var index=0;
	   for (var i = 0; i < p.children.length; i++) {
	    	   if (p.children.item(i) == tr) {
	    	     index = i;
	    	     break;
	    	   }
	   }
       var rowCount=0
       if(nestCount >0){
	      rowCount=parseInt(index);//root question index added here
	      for(var i=index; i<= rowCount; i++) {
		      if(tBody.rows[i]!=null){
                  var subQuestionCount = juic.$('addQuest2Req_subquestion_count' + quesIndex);
                  if (subQuestionCount && subQuestionCount.value && subQuestionCount.value > 0) {
                      rowCount = rowCount + parseInt(subQuestionCount.value);//adding next level parent sub questions count
                  }
		          tBody.deleteRow(i);
		          qlist = qlist+''+quesIndex+',';
		          quesIndex++;
		       	  rowCount--;
		          i--;
			   }
		   }
       } else {
    	 qlist = qlist+''+questionId+',';
    	 p.removeChild(tr);
       }
       // deleteTableRow(tr);
     }
     document.getElementById('addQuest2Req_deleted_quest').value = qlist;

     var questTable = document.getElementById('selectedQuestions');
     refreshStyles(questTable);
     var tbody = questTable.getElementsByTagName("TBODY");
     // var count = --insertQuestIndex; //tbody[0].childNodes.length;
     // document.getElementById('addQuest2Req_num_of_quest').value = count;

   }

   return input_entry;
 }

 function validateQuestion(value, placeHolderId) {
    if(value.trim() == "") {
        alert('Please enter your question.');
        return false;
    } else if (placeHolderId){
      document.getElementById(placeHolderId).textContent = value;
      document.getElementById(placeHolderId).innerText = value;
      document.getElementById(placeHolderId).text = value;
    }
    return true;
 }


  function addQuestions(tabName) {
    var localIds = '', publicIds = '';
    if (tabName == "add_q_from_search") {
       localIds = document.getElementById('selected_in_local').value;
       publicIds = document.getElementById('selected_in_search').value;
       addPubQuestion(publicIds,false);
       addLocalQuestion(localIds,false);

       document.getElementById('selected_in_local').value = "";
       document.getElementById('selected_in_search').value = "";
       var addBttonFromSearch = document.getElementsByName('add_q_from_search')[0];
       if(addBttonFromSearch){
           addBttonFromSearch.setAttribute('disabled','false');
       }
    } else if (tabName == "add_q_from_browse") {
       localIds = document.getElementById('selected_in_local').value;
       publicIds = document.getElementById('selected_in_browse').value;
       addPubQuestion(publicIds,true);
       addLocalQuestion(localIds,true);
       document.getElementById('selected_in_local').value = "";
       document.getElementById('selected_in_browse').value = "";
       document.getElementById('selected_in_local').value = "";
       document.getElementById('selected_in_browse').value = "";
       var addBttonFrombrowse = document.getElementsByName('add_q_from_browse')[0];
       if(addBttonFrombrowse){
           addBttonFrombrowse.setAttribute('disabled','false');
       }
    }
    var questions = [].concat(localIds.split(','), publicIds.split(','));
    var questionsNumber = 0;
    questions.forEach(function(questionId) {
      if (questionId.length > 0) {
        questionsNumber++;
      }
    });
    var questionsSROnlyElement = document.getElementById('questions-sr-only-notify');
    if (questionsNumber > 0 && questionsSROnlyElement) {
      questionsSROnlyElement.innerText = sfMessageFormat.format(questionsNumber === 1 ? "1 question was added to the Questions list" : "{0} questions were added to the Questions list", questionsNumber);
      setTimeout(() => {
        questionsSROnlyElement.innerText = '';
      }, 100);
    }
    var count = 0;
    if(insertQuestIndex > 0){
      if(nestItems){
        count = insertQuestIndex - nestItems.length;
      }else{
        count = insertQuestIndex - questionsNumber;
      }
    }
    var el = juic.$(count+'answer1_menu_answerLink');
    if(el){
      el.focus();
    }
    Util.fdPostProcess();
  }

 function setChanged(questionIndex) {
    var answerChanged = juic.$('addQuest2Req_anwser_changed' + questionIndex);
    answerChanged.value = "true";
    var addedOrModifiedQuestionList = juic.$('addQuest2Req_added_or_modified_quest');
    var changeList = (addedOrModifiedQuestionList.value) ? addedOrModifiedQuestionList.value.split(',') : [];
    changeList.push(questionIndex);
    addedOrModifiedQuestionList.value = changeList.join(',');
 }

 function resetChanged(questionIndex) {
     var addedOrModifiedQuestionList = juic.$('addQuest2Req_added_or_modified_quest');
     if (addedOrModifiedQuestionList && addedOrModifiedQuestionList.value) {
        var changeList = addedOrModifiedQuestionList.value.split(",");
        var index = changeList.indexOf(questionIndex);
        if (index > -1) {
            changeList.splice(index, 1);
        }
        addedOrModifiedQuestionList.value = changeList.join(',');
      }

     // we set false only if all of the options are the same as they were on page load
     // changList has all occurrences of changes to a question; Maximum three changes
     var answerChanged = juic.$('addQuest2Req_anwser_changed' + questionIndex);
     if (changeList.indexOf(questionIndex) < 0) {
        // if there are no changes for the questionIndex; then set answerChange to false
        answerChanged.value = "false";
      }
  }

  // Added this method to check if the value is changed or not.
  // options.oldValue contains the original value.
  function isValueChanged(questionIndex, obj, options) {
    if(!options || options.oldValue === undefined) {
      return;
    }
    var changed = false;
    if (obj.type == "checkbox") {
        changed = obj.checked != options.oldValue;
    } else {
        changed = obj.value != options.oldValue;
    }
    if (changed) {
        setChanged(questionIndex);
    } else {
        resetChanged(questionIndex);
    }
  }

  function addPubQuestion(pubQids,isBrowseTabAction) {
	 // Added this if condition to differentate the actions for browse and search functions
	 // as question retrieval based on user selected locale is not required for search
	   var local =(isBrowseTabAction == true)?encodeURIComponent(rcmQuestionLanguages.getSelectedLanguage()) : encodeURIComponent('en_GB'); // fix for RCM-12683
     var url = "/rcmjsup?m=getPubQuestionDetail&qIds=";
     var timeStamp = new Date().getTime();
     url = url+pubQids+"&locale="+local+"&invalidateCache="+timeStamp+"&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey;
     addPageAction(RecruitingActionType.GET_PUB_QUESTION_DETAIL);
     if (submitAjaxQuery(url)) {
        if(queried_items > 0) {
           nestItems=items;
           for(var i = 0; i < items.length; i++){
              // each item should be a FMQuestion
              var question = items[i];
              addSelectedQuestion(question,false);
              uncheckQuestions('pub', pubQids);
           }
        } //end for
     }
  }

  function addLocalQuestion(localIds,isBrowseTabAction) {
	// Added this if condition to differentate the actions for browse and search functions
    // as question retrieval based on user selected locale is not required for search
    var local =(isBrowseTabAction == true)?encodeURIComponent(rcmQuestionLanguages.getSelectedLanguage()) : null; // fix for RCM-12683
    var url = "/rcmjsup?m=getLocalQuestionDetail&qIds=";
    url = url+localIds+"&locale="+local+"&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey;
     addPageAction(RecruitingActionType.GET_LOCAL_QUESTION_DETAIL);
     if (submitAjaxQuery(url)) {
        if(queried_items > 0) {
           for(var i = 0; i < items.length; i++){
              // each item should be a FMQuestion
              var question = items[i];
              addSelectedQuestion(question,false);
              uncheckQuestions('loc', localIds);
           } //end for
        }
     }
  }

  function uncheckQuestions(type, ids) {
    idList = ids.split(',');
    for (var i=0; i < idList.length; i++) {
        if (idList[i] != "") {
          var eid = 'stab'+type+idList[i];
          elem = document.getElementById(eid);
          if(elem) {
            elem.checked = false;
          }
          eid = 'btab'+type+idList[i];
          elem = document.getElementById(eid);
          if (elem) {
            elem.checked = false;
          }
        }
    }
  }

  // load the answer section for create new question tab
   function loadNewAnswer(){
   var newAnswerDiv = document.getElementById("newAnswerDivId");
   newAnswerDiv.innerHTML == ""

    var url = "/rcmjsup?m=includeFBAnswer";
    url += "&insertIndex=" + insertQuestIndex + "&questionType='jobReq'&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey;

    prepareAjaxRequest();
    if (req) {
      try {
        req.open("GET", url, false);
        req.send(null);

        if (req.status != 200) {
          alert("Status "+req.status);
          error_text = req.statusText;
        }

        newAnswerDiv.innerHTML = req.responseText;

      } catch (e) {
        error_text = e.message;
      }
    } // end if (req)

 }
   //Expands the parent question to display child questions.
   function expandQuestion(id,obj,subQuestionsCount){
	  juic.$("close_selectedQuestion"+id).style.display="inline";
    juic.$("close_selectedQuestion"+id).style.height="auto";
	  juic.$("open_selectedQuestion"+id).style.display="none";
    if (Util.isFioriFDEnabled()) {
	    juic.$("close_selectedQuestion"+id).style.display="inline-flex";
    }
		   tr = findParent(obj, "TR");
		   if (tr){
		       p = findParent(obj, "TBODY");
		       index=0;
			   for (var i = 0; i < p.rows.length; i++) {
			    if (p.rows[i] == tr) {
			     index = i;
			     break;
			     }
			   }
		       tBody=  findParent(obj, "TBODY");
			   rowCount=parseInt(index)+parseInt(subQuestionsCount);
			   for(i=index+1; i<=rowCount; i++){
			     row = tBody.rows[i];
			     row.style.display="table-row";
			    }
		      }
          juic.$("close_selectedQuestion"+id).focus();
	      }
  //Collapses the parent to hide the child questions.
  function collapseQuestion(id,obj,subQuestionsCount){
	   juic.$("open_selectedQuestion"+id).style.display="inline";
     juic.$("open_selectedQuestion"+id).style.height="auto";
	   juic.$("close_selectedQuestion"+id).style.display="none";
     if (Util.isFioriFDEnabled()) {
      juic.$("open_selectedQuestion"+id).style.display="inline-flex";
     }
		   tr = findParent(obj, "TR");
		   if (tr) {
		    p = findParent(obj, "TBODY");
		    index=0;
		   for (var i = 0; i < p.rows.length; i++){
			 if (p.rows[i] == tr){
			   index = i;
			   break;
			  }
			}
		    tBody=  findParent(obj, "TBODY");
		    rowCount=parseInt(index)+parseInt(subQuestionsCount);
			for(var i=index+1; i<=rowCount; i++){
			 row = tBody.rows[i];
			  row.style.display='none';

			}
		  }
      juic.$("open_selectedQuestion"+id).focus();
	  }
  function addSelectedQuestion(question,isCreateQuestionAction) {
    var questTable = document.getElementById('selectedQuestions');
    var tbody = questTable.getElementsByTagName("TBODY");
    var count = insertQuestIndex; //tbody[0].childNodes.length;
    var newTr = document.createElement("tr");
    var expandTd = document.createElement("td");
    var nameTd = document.createElement("td");
    var nameTdDiv = document.createElement("div");
    var cascadeTd = document.createElement("td");
   if(question.questionParentId>0)
   {   newTr.className = "a hide";
       cascadeTd.colSpan = "7";
   }else{
	   newTr.className = "a";
   }
    newTr.id = "selectedQuestion"+count;
 	// Added this if condition to append the Parent Answer
    // before the sub question
    if(question.questionParentId>0){
    	var parentAnswerSpan = document.createElement("span");
    	parentAnswerSpan.innerText = "[\""+question.questionParentResponse+"\"]";
    	parentAnswerSpan.textContent = "[\""+question.questionParentResponse+"\"]";
    	var spaceElement = document.createTextNode('\u00A0');
       	nameTdDiv.appendChild(parentAnswerSpan);
       	nameTdDiv.appendChild(spaceElement);
    }
    else if(question.questionParentId < 0 && question.subQuestionsAvailable == "true"){
    	var parentQuestionSpan = document.createElement("span");
    	parentQuestionSpan.className ="cascade_collapseicon";
    	var collapse_icon =document.createElement("a");
    	collapse_icon.id = "open_selectedQuestion"+count;
    	collapse_icon.className = "arrow_open sapIcon " + Util.generateFDClasses("link");
      collapse_icon.tabIndex = "0";
      collapse_icon.role= "button";
		  collapse_icon.ariaLabel = "Collapsed. To expand press enter.";
    	collapse_icon.href = "javascript:void(0)";
    	collapse_icon.innerHTML="&#xe1f6;";
    	collapse_icon.onclick =	function() {expandQuestion(count,this,question.subQuestionsCount);};

    	parentQuestionSpan.appendChild(collapse_icon);

   		var collapse_icon1 =document.createElement("a");
    	collapse_icon1.id = "close_selectedQuestion"+count;
    	collapse_icon1.className = "arrow_close hide sapIcon " + Util.generateFDClasses("link");
      collapse_icon1.tabIndex = "0";
      collapse_icon1.role= "button";
      collapse_icon1.ariaLabel = "Expanded. To collapse press enter.";
    	collapse_icon1.href = "javascript:void(0)";
    	collapse_icon1.innerHTML="&#xe1f7;";
    	collapse_icon1.onclick = function() {collapseQuestion(count,this,question.subQuestionsCount);};

    	parentQuestionSpan.appendChild(collapse_icon1);
    	expandTd.appendChild(parentQuestionSpan);

    }

    var placeHolder = document.createElement("span");
    placeHolder.id = "question"+count+"Placeholder";
    placeHolder.className = "questionPlaceholder";
    var qName = document.createTextNode(question.questionName + " ");
    placeHolder.appendChild(qName);
    if(question.questionParentId>0){
    	nameTdDiv.className = "CascadingIndent";
    }
    nameTdDiv.appendChild(placeHolder);

    var editQuest = document.createElement("span");
    editQuest.id =  "question"+count+"Edit";
    editQuest.className = "hide sfTextAreaWrapper";
    var editArea = document.createElement("textArea");
    editArea.id = "question"+count+"EditField";
    editArea.className = Util.generateFDClasses("textarea sfTextArea");
    editArea.name = "addQuest2Req_question_name_"+count;
    editArea.NAME = "addQuest2Req_question_name_"+count;
    editArea.style.size = "40";
    editArea.style.rows = "3";
    editArea.onblur = function(event) {
        validateQuestion(this.value,  placeHolder.id);
        showHideLayers( placeHolder.id, editQuest.id ,'inline');
    };
    editArea.onkeypress = function(event) {
        if (event.keyCode == 13) {
            validateQuestion(this.value,  placeHolder.id);
            showHideLayers( placeHolder.id, editQuest.id ,'inline');
            SFDom.setFocus("question" + count + "Menu_select", true); //Focus the select button
        }
    };
    var qNameEdit = document.createTextNode(question.questionName);
    editArea.appendChild(qNameEdit);
    editQuest.appendChild(editArea);
    nameTdDiv.appendChild(editQuest);

      if(questionTypeSel){
        var questionType = questionTypeSel.options[questionTypeSel.selectedIndex].text;
        if(question.questionParentId <0){
        	if (questionType == jsMessages["QUESTION_TEXT"]) {
          checkBox1.disabled = false;
          checkBox2.disabled = true;
          checkBox3.disabled = true;
          weight.disabled = true;
        } else if (questionType == jsMessages["QUESTION_NO_ANSWER"]) {
          checkBox1.disabled = true;
          checkBox2.disabled = true;
          checkBox3.disabled = true;
          weight.disabled = true;
        } else {
          checkBox1.disabled = false;
          checkBox2.disabled = false;
          checkBox3.disabled = false;
          weight.disabled = false;
        }
        }
        var hrefText = document.createTextNode(questionType);
        editAnswerHref.appendChild(hrefText);
      } else {
        alert('No answer menu');
      }
      if (browserDetector.isIE && Util.ieVersion() < 10) {
      invi(count + 'answer_div',0);
      var newAnswerDiv = document.getElementById("newAnswerDivId");
      nameTd.innerHTML += newAnswerDiv.innerHTML;
      newAnswerDiv.innerHTML = "";
    } else {
	    var newAnswerDiv = document.getElementById(count + 'answer_div');

	    if(newAnswerDiv){
	      invi(newAnswerDiv.id, 0);
	      nameTd.appendChild(newAnswerDiv);
	    }
    }
    }
    insertQuestIndex++;
    loadNewAnswer();
    if(question.questionType == 'QUESTION_RATING') {
      wireShowScaleDetail('scale_'+count);
    }
    return false;
    Util.fdPostProcess();
  }

  function searchByKeyword(noResult ) {
    keyword = document.getElementById('addQuest2Req_keyword').value;
    var url = "/rcmjsup?m=searchQuestionsByKeyword&contentId=";
    url = url+encodeURIComponent(keyword);
    url += "&locale="+encodeURIComponent('en_GB');
    url += "&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey;
    addPageAction(RecruitingActionType.SEARCH_QUESTIONS_BY_KEYWORD);
    if (submitAjaxQuery(url)) {
        if(queried_items > 0) {

           var divSect = document.getElementById('searchResults');
           divSect.innerHTML = "";
           var hrElem = document.createElement("hr");
           hrElem.className = "toppad5";
           divSect.appendChild(hrElem);
           var h4Elem = document.createElement("h4");
           h4Elem.className = "clear_none";
           var label = document.createTextNode('Search Results:');
           h4Elem.appendChild(label);
           divSect.appendChild(h4Elem);
           var qNameDiv = document.createElement("div");
           for(var i = 0; i < items.length; i++){
              // each item should be a FMQuestion
              var question = items[i];

              // Added this if condition to filtering the top level
              // questions displaying on the UI
              if(question.questionParentId <0) {
            	  cbColumn = document.createElement("div");
                  cbColumn.className = "checkbox_column browseLineItem";
                  cbColumn.role = "listitem";
                  var cb = document.createElement("input");
                  cb.type = "checkbox";
                  cb.className = Util.generateFDClasses("checkbox");
                  cb.name = "addQuest2Req_selectedQuest"+i;
                  cb.id = question.questionId;
                  cb.ariaLabel = question.questionName + ' ' + sfMessageFormat.format("{0} of {1}", i + 1, items.length);
                  if (question.isPublic) {
                    cb.id = 'stabpub'+question.questionId;
                    cb.onclick = function() {
                       addQuestion(this.id, this.checked,'selected_in_search');
                   };
                  } else {
                    cb.id = 'stabloc'+question.questionId;
                    cb.onclick = function() {
                       addQuestion(this.id, this.checked,'selected_in_local');
                   };
                  }
                  cbColumn.appendChild(cb);
                  var qLabel = document.createElement("label");
                  qLabel.className = Util.generateFDClasses("checkbox__label");
                  qLabel.setAttribute("for", (question.isPublic ? 'stabpub' : 'stabloc') + question.questionId);
                  var qLabelText = document.createElement("span");
                  qLabelText.className = Util.generateFDClasses("checkbox__text");
                  qLabelText.innerText = question.questionName;
                  qLabel.appendChild(qLabelText);

              }
              // Added this if condition to show the Cascade Image only
              // if the top level question has sub questions
              if(question.subQuestionsAvailable == "true"){
              	 var cascadeImg = document.createElement("span");
              	cascadeImg.className = "smallIconPadding bottompad5 cascadeIconSpan sapIcon";
              	cascadeImg.innerHTML ='&#xe0d1;';
              	cascadeImg.title = "Cascaded Question";
              	cascadeImg.style.margin = "0px 0px 0px 5px";
                qLabel.appendChild(cascadeImg);
               }
               cbColumn.appendChild(qLabel);
               divSect.appendChild(cbColumn);
           } //end for
           divBtn = document.createElement("div");
           divBtn.className = "clear_all";
           searchBtn = document.createElement("input");
           searchBtn.type = "button";
           searchBtn.disabled="false";
           searchBtn.className = "globalSecondaryButton " + Util.generateFDClasses("button");
           searchBtn.name = "add_q_from_search" ;
           searchBtn.NAME = "add_q_from_search" ;
           searchBtn.value = 'Add';
           searchBtn.onclick = function() {
                   addQuestions('add_q_from_search');
                   return false;
               };
           searchBtn.onkeydown = function(e) {
             var keycode = e.which || e.keyCode || e.charCode;
             if(e.type=='keydown' && (keycode==SFDOMEvent.KEY_CODE.RETURN || keycode==SFDOMEvent.KEY_CODE.SPACE)) {
               addQuestions('add_q_from_search');
             }
           };
           divBtn.appendChild(searchBtn);
           divSect.appendChild(divBtn);
        }
       else {
	     var divSect = document.getElementById('searchResults');
		  divSect.innerHTML =  noResult  ;
	     }
     }
     Util.fdPostProcess();
  }

  function createAdhoc() {
     var question = new Object();
     question.questionName = document.getElementById('create_question_name').value;
     question.questionId = -1;
     question.questionParentId = -1;
     addSelectedQuestion(question,true);
     document.getElementById('create_question_name').value = "";
     Util.fdPostProcess();
  }
  
  function addTabindexCaptionToQuestionsTable(){
    var domCaption = document.createElement("caption");
    domCaption.className = "sr-only";
    domCaption.innerHTML = "Questions";
  
    var elementInterval = window.setInterval(function(){
	var $el = juic.$('selectedQuestions') || null;

	if($el){
	    /* Commenting out this line of code as per
         * Accessibility standards: tables should not have tabindexes.
         */
        //$el.tabIndex = 0;
        $el.appendChild(domCaption);
		clearInterval(elementInterval);
      }
	},100);
  }
  
  addTabindexCaptionToQuestionsTable();

 function loadAnswerForQuestion(id, insertId, qid, isPublic) {
   var answerDiv = document.getElementById(id);
   answerDiv.innerHTML == ""
    addPageAction(RecruitingActionType.LOAD_ANSWER_FOR_QUESTIONS);
    var url = "/rcmjsup?m=includeFBAnswer";
    url += "&insertIndex=" + insertId + "&questionType=jobReq"+"&isPublic="+isPublic +"&locale="+encodeURIComponent(rcmQuestionLanguages.getSelectedLanguage());
    if(qid){
      url += "&questionId="+qid;
    }
    var jobReqSelectedLocale = document.getElementById('jobReqSelectedLocale');
    var jobReqDefaultLocale = document.getElementById('jobReqDefaultLocale');
    if(jobReqSelectedLocale && jobReqDefaultLocale) {
        url += "&jobReqSelectedLocale="+jobReqSelectedLocale.value;
        url += "&jobReqDefaultLocale="+jobReqDefaultLocale.value;
    }
    url += "&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey;
    prepareAjaxRequest();
    if (req) {
      try {
        req.open("GET", url, false);
        req.send(null);

        if (req.status != 200) {
          alert("Status "+req.status);
          error_text = req.statusText;
        }

        answerDiv.innerHTML = req.responseText;

      } catch (e) {
        error_text = e.message;
      }
    } // end if (req)
  }

  function showNewAnswerDiv(event){
    if (event && event.target) {
      event.target.ariaExpanded = 'true';
    }
    invi(insertQuestIndex + 'answer_div', 1);
  }
  function loadLanguages(){
    var config = { fieldDescription : "Select language" };
    rcmQuestionLanguages = new RcmQuestionLanguages('en_GB',[{"key":"All","value":"All"},{"key":"English UK ‎(English UK)‎","value":"en_GB"},{"key":"Français ‎(French)‎","value":"fr_FR"}], config);
    rcmQuestionLanguages.render("questionLanguages");
  }
  
    function handleSelectKeyDown(index, event) {
        if (event && (event.type === "click" || event.keyCode === 13 || event.keyCode === 32)) {
            SFDOMEvent.preventDefault(event);
            invi("question" + index + "Menu", true);
            SFDom.setFocus("editQuestion" + index + "Link", true);
        }
    }

    function handleMenuKeyDown(index, event) {
        var deleteRef = "deleteQuestion" + index + "Link";
        var editRef = "editQuestion" + index + "Link";
        var hideQuestRef = "hideQuestion" + index + "DescLink";
        var showQuestRef= "showQuestion" + index + "DescLink";
        if (event) {
          switch(event.keyCode) {
            case SFDOMEvent.KEY_CODE.ESCAPE:
              var menuId = "question" + index + "Menu";
              invi(menuId, false);
              SFDom.setFocus(menuId + "_select", true);
              break;
            
            case SFDOMEvent.KEY_CODE.ARROW_UP:
              SFDOMEvent.preventDefault(event);
              switch(event.target.id)	{
              case editRef:
                  SFDom.setFocus(deleteRef);
                  break;
              case showQuestRef:
              case hideQuestRef:					
                  SFDom.setFocus(editRef);
                  break;
              case deleteRef:
                  if(juic.$(showQuestRef).style && juic.$(showQuestRef).style.cssText == 'display: none;') {
                    SFDom.setFocus(hideQuestRef);
                  } else {
                    SFDom.setFocus(showQuestRef);
                  }
                  break;					
              }
            break;				
            case SFDOMEvent.KEY_CODE.ARROW_DOWN:
              SFDOMEvent.preventDefault(event);
              switch(event.target.id)	{
              case editRef:
                  if(juic.$(showQuestRef).style && juic.$(showQuestRef).style.cssText == 'display: none;') {
                    SFDom.setFocus(hideQuestRef);
                  } else {
                    SFDom.setFocus(showQuestRef);
                  }
                  break;
              case showQuestRef:
              case hideQuestRef:					
                  SFDom.setFocus(deleteRef);
                  break;				
              case deleteRef:
                  SFDom.setFocus(editRef);
                  break;					
              }
            break;
          }
        }
    }
-->

				<script type="text/javascript">
					RCMElementsUtil.find('#show-rating-scales0sel_scale_detail_div').on("click keydown",function(e){						
						var keycode = e.which || e.keyCode || e.charCode;
						if(keycode!=32 && keycode!=13 && e.type=='keydown') return;
				        SFDOMEvent.preventDefault(e); // use this instead of e.preventDefault() to handle problems with IE8
						RCMElementsUtil.$new(this).hide();
						RCMElementsUtil.find('#0sel_scale_detail_div').show();
						RCMElementsUtil.find('#hide-rating-scales0sel_scale_detail_div').show().focus();
					});
					RCMElementsUtil.find('#hide-rating-scales0sel_scale_detail_div').on("click keydown",function(e){						
						var keycode = e.which || e.keyCode || e.charCode;
						if(keycode!=32 && keycode!=13 && e.type=='keydown') return;						
		                SFDOMEvent.preventDefault(e); // use this instead of e.preventDefault() to handle problems with IE8
						RCMElementsUtil.find("#show-rating-scales0sel_scale_detail_div").show().focus();
						RCMElementsUtil.find("#0sel_scale_detail_div,#hide-rating-scales0sel_scale_detail_div").hide()
					});
          var tabs = document.querySelectorAll("#questions ul.axial_tabs li");
					for (var i=0; i<tabs.length; i++){
					    tabs[i].addEventListener('keydown', arroKeyNavigation);
					};
          setTimeout(() => {
            var questionDom = juic.$("0questionPlaceholder");
            if(questionDom) {
              var questionText = questionDom.innerText + " " + jsMessages.ANSWER_FORMAT;
            };
            var answerRegion = juic.$("0answer_div");
            if (answerRegion) {
              answerRegion.setAttribute("aria-label", questionText);
            };
          }, 900);
        
					function arroKeyNavigation(event){
						switch (SFDOMEvent.getKeyName(event)) {
							case 'ARROWLEFT':
							case 'ARROWUP' :
								event.preventDefault();
								setFocusBackward(getIndex(event.currentTarget.id));
						    break;
						
              case 'ARROWRIGHT':
              case 'ARROWDOWN':
								event.preventDefault();
								setFocusForward(getIndex(event.currentTarget.id));
						    break;
              case 'RETURN' :
						  case 'SPACEBAR' :
                event.preventDefault();
								event.srcElement.lastElementChild.click();
							default:
						    break;
						}
					};
					function setFocusForward(idx){
					  if(idx < tabs.length-1){
						  juic.$(tabs[idx]).setAttribute("tabindex","-1");
						  juic.$(tabs[idx+1]).setAttribute("tabindex","0");
						  SFDom.setFocus(juic.$(tabs[idx+1].id));
						}
					};
					function setFocusBackward(idx){
					  if(idx > 0){
						  juic.$(tabs[idx]).setAttribute("tabindex","-1");
						  juic.$(tabs[idx-1]).setAttribute("tabindex","0");
						  SFDom.setFocus(juic.$(tabs[idx-1].id));
						}
					};
					function getIndex(currentTabId){
						var indx = null;
						for(var i=0; i<tabs.length; i++){
							if (currentTabId === tabs[i].id){
								indx = i;
							}
						}
						return indx;
					};
				</script>

<script>

function closeAnswerRange(element,e){
	var $self = RCMElementsUtil.$(element);	
	var keyCode = e.keyCode || e.charCode || e.which;
  if(e.type=="keydown" && keyCode==9 && e.shiftKey){
    if($self.skipOut(3).find(".answer-format-combobox").val()=='QUESTION_RATING'){
		  e.preventDefault();
		  $self.skipOut(3).find(".rating-scales-radio-button-group").focus();
    }
		return;
  }
	if(e.type=="keydown" && (keyCode!=32 && keyCode!=13)) return;	
	e.preventDefault();
	$self.skipOut(5).hide();
	var expandButton = $self.skipOut(7).find(".click-to-set");
	expandButton.attr("aria-expanded", "false");
	$self.skipOut(7).find(".click-to-set").focus();
}
</script>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">


function attachToolTip(elementType) {
    var els = document.getElementsByTagName(elementType);
    var pageInfo = window.pageHeaderJsonData && window.pageHeaderJsonData.pageInfo;
    var pageQualifier = pageInfo && pageInfo.pageQualifier;
    for (var e = 0, n=els.length; e < n ; e++) {
            els[e]._title = els[e].title; // To prevent default tooltip from showing
            if(els[e].disabled){
            els[e].title = Util.unescapeHTML(els[e].title); // To prevent default tooltip from showing escaped character. Since custom tooltip will not work on disabled field. 
            }
          if(pageQualifier != "JOB_REQ_DETAIL" && pageQualifier != "CAREERS_VIEW_JOB_APPLICATION") {  
            if (els[e]._title !== "") {
              els[e].onmouseover = function() {
                  if(this.title !== ""){
                      this._title = this.title; // if saved value of the mandatory field is deleted, show that field is required in custom tooltip. 
                  }                                     
                  showToolTip(this,this._title);
                  this.setAttribute('title','');
              };
            } 
          }
    }
}

if(picklist && !picklist._paginatedPicklist) {
  chain(window, "onload", picklist.attachBehaviors);
}

function createToolTip() {
    var elementTypes = ["select","input","textarea","span","div"];
    for (var eleIdx=0; eleIdx < elementTypes.length; eleIdx++ ) {
        attachToolTip(elementTypes[eleIdx]);
    }
}

SFDOMEvent.ready(createToolTip);

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

  function preventSubmissionOnEnterKey() {
      var jrRendererPage = document.getElementsByClassName("formSectionBody");
      if (jrRendererPage && jrRendererPage[0]){
          SFDOMEvent.addListener(jrRendererPage[0], "keypress", function(event) {
              var key = SFDOMEvent.getKeyName(event);
              if (key == 'RETURN' && event.target.tagName.toLowerCase()!= "textarea"){
                 event.preventDefault();
              }
          });
      }
  }
  SFDOMEvent.ready(preventSubmissionOnEnterKey);
  
  if (typeof competencyInputFieldId !== 'undefined') {
	  SFDOMEvent.ready(_loadAttributes);
  }

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">


/* 
 * This function finds all the (div class="commentsArea") which wraps fb_sect_ui_comments.jsp
 * and adds a target="_new", unless the tag starts with "javascript:" like spellchecker, legal scan
 * and waca. Also doesn't add the new target attribute if the tags parent className is "textAreaControls"
 * which happens when rich text editor is turned off and spellchecker, legal scan and waca are all
 * hyperlinks (anchor tags).
 */

var isCheckedCommentsArea = false; 
 
window.addEventListener("load",function() {
  if (isCheckedCommentsArea){
    return;
  }
  isCheckedCommentsArea = true;
  
  var cBoxes = SFDom.getElementsByClassName("commentsArea", "div");
  for (var i=0,len=cBoxes.length;i<len;++i) {
    var tags = cBoxes[i].getElementsByTagName("a");
	    for (var x=0,l=tags.length;x<l;++x) {
	    	if(tags[x].href.indexOf("javascript:") == -1){
	    		if(tags[x].parentNode.className != "textAreaControls"){
	      	 		tags[x].setAttribute("target","_new");
	      	 	}
	        }
	    }
  }
});

</script>

  function saveForm() {

      form.submit();
    }
  }

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">


var openSC_next_function;

function openRSSpellCheck(finishFunc) {
  self.openSC_next_function = finishFunc;
  setTimeout(function () { // PLT-16336 Timeout needed in iOS to allow the current popup window that invoked this function to close before another popup is opened via this code.
      rswm_RunSpellCheck(true);
  }, 500);
}

function spellCheckDone() {
  if(openSC_next_function) {
    setTimeout(openSC_next_function, 500); // PLT-16336 Timeout needed in iOS to allow the current popup window that invoked this function to close before another popup is opened via this code
  }
   
  self.openSC_next_function = null;
}

function openLegalScanFormLater(formDataId, finishFunc){
  setTimeout(function () { // PLT-16336 Timeout needed in iOS to allow the current popup window that invoked this function to close before another popup is opened via this code
      openLegalScanForm(formDataId, finishFunc);
  }, 500);
}

</script>




<script type="text/javascript">


showWeightErrorMessage();
  
function showWeightErrorMessage() {
  if (true) { //option=error
    alert("Please correct the following error(s):\n\nStaffing process is a required field.\n");
  }
  else {  //option=warning
    var msg =  "";
    msg += "Click \u2018OK\u2019 to ignore this warning and continue with your action, or click \u2018Cancel\u2019 to cancel the action and fix the problems.";
    if (confirm(msg)) {
      document.getElementById("skip_weight_validate").value = 'true';
      if (true) {
        var routingBarOptionField = gebi('fb2rte_option');
        if (routingBarOptionField != null) {
          setField('fb2rte_option','100011297_inner_step_send');
          routingBarOptionField.disabled=false; //enable hidden field for submit
        }
        
        // EE-13994: Need to add additional field for submitting.
        
        
      }
      document.forms[0].submit();
    }
    else {
      return false;
    }
  }
}

</script>
